type='text'>&quot;Kawasaki Ninja 250cc Strong and silent wins the race&quot;</title><content type='html'>&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;FEW motorcycles boast true dual-purpose capabilities.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Some are good road bikes, but once the terrain gets loose with gravel or dirt, such bikes can&#39;t cope.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The 2010 Kawasaki KLX 250 is an exception.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This lean and green dirt machine will swallow open roads while tackling some off-road madness at the same time.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Just ask the Royal Malaysian Police based in Johor Baru.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Its Ninja Squad, tasked to nab robbers or traffic offenders, is equipped with the formidable 250cc KLX dirtbikes.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The squad has been successfully catching fleeing offenders, all thanks to the flexibility of the KLX 250.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It&#39;s agile in the streets and also over obstacles like stairs or even potholes found on dirt tracks.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;With a 135kg wet weight (fully fuelled), the slim KLX is light, perfect for handling corners.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Making steering corrections while the KLX is tipped over in bumpy corners becomes a forgiving exercise.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Its low seat height also means that most riders will not be tip-toeing.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This boosts confidence and makes the KLX easier to ride compared to more focused dirtbikes.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Its dual-purpose tyres ensures that it can perform road duties and some intermediate off-road riding.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Other factors, like its smooth power delivery, make the electric start Kawasaki stand out.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Its six-speed gearbox doesn&#39;t stutter when the bike accelerates.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;When ridden below 6,000rpm, it feels as though you&#39;re riding an automatic scooter, allowing you to lazily chug along city streets.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The almost silent exhaust will deceive newbies into thinking that the KLX is impotent.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Get the revs over the 7,000rpm mark and the engine starts to sing with urgency.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Higher up the rev range is where the KLX makes most of its power before hitting its 10,500rpm redline on the digital dash.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To squeeze every ounce of performance on fast trails, the bike should be ridden with the throttle wide open.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;But don&#39;t expect any body-jolting torque from the KLX.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;After all, it&#39;s only a 250cc bike.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Still, its suspension is perfectly tuned for the road as you will barely notice bumps that you have ridden over.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In off-road situations, some fine-tuning is required.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;We increased the front and rear rebound damping to calm the KLX when the bike was ridden hard off-road.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The brakes on the KLX has a more progressive feel to them, unlike other braking systems which have a stronger initial bite when the brakes are activated.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Naturally, there are trade-offs compared to bigger capacity dirtbikes.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A medium-sized bike like the KLX has excellent mileage, unlike its bigger fuel-guzzling siblings.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;But getting a little more oomph from the futuristic-looking KLX, which is equipped with pointed headlights and brakelights, will not be difficult.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Just add an aftermarket, slip-on exhaust pipe and you&#39;ll likely see some increase to the KLX&#39;s mid-range performance.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Another way is to replace its current 42-tooth rear sprocket with a bigger one.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This will give it more boost during acceleration, but at the expense of some top speed.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In its standard form, the KLX will cruise at 100kmh at 6,500rpm in sixth gear.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Top speed is in the range of 120kmh.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;And its 7.6litre fuel capacity is claimed to be good for 220km.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://www.kawasakimotorcycle.org/images/2010/Ninja250R.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;2010 Kawasaki NinjaÂ® 250R&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;280&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;</content><link rel='replies' type='application/atom+xml' Sweden Industry Guide&lt;/a&gt;&quot; report to their offering. &lt;p&gt; The &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://cts.businesswire.com/ct/CT?id=smartlink&amp;amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F8b0c45%2Fautomotive_sweden&amp;amp;esheet=6217353&amp;amp;lan=en_US&amp;amp;anchor=Automotive%3A+Sweden+Industry+Guide&amp;amp;index=3&amp;amp;md5=8ea18780596861ff09d1ff8945712d58&quot;&gt;Automotive: Sweden Industry Guide&lt;/a&gt; is an essential resource for top-level data and analysis covering the Sweden Automotive industry. It includes detailed data on market size and segmentation, textual analysis of the key trends and competitive landscape, and profiles of the leading companies. This incisive report provides expert analysis with distinct chapters for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, New Cars and Trucks. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Scope of the Report &lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;Contains an executive summary and data on value, volume and segmentation for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, New Cars and Trucks &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Provides textual analysis of the industry&#39;s prospects, competitive landscape and profiles of the leading companies &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Incorporates in-depth five forces competitive environment analysis and scorecards &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Includes five-year forecasts for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, New Cars and Trucks &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt; Highlights &lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;The Swedish trucks market generated total revenues of $1.4 billion in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -3.5% for the period spanning 2005-2009. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;The Swedish light trucks market generated total revenues of $556.4 million in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -7.4% for the period spanning 2005-2009. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;The Swedish medium and heavy trucks market generated total revenues of $817.8 million in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -0.3% for the period spanning 2005-2009. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;The Swedish motorcycles market generated total revenues of $251.1 million in 2008, representing a compound annual growth rate (CAGR) of 9.6% for the period spanning 2004-2008. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;The Swedish new cars market generated total revenues of $5.4 billion in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -5.9% for the period spanning 2005-2009. &lt;/li&gt; href=&quot;http://www.fredericksburg.com/News/FLS/2010/032010/03172010/534870&quot;&gt;Local man charged in six city burglaries - Free Lance-Star&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 16 Mar 2010 09:33 PM PDT&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;p&gt;   &lt;/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Man caught on surveillance camera charged with multiple burglaries. &lt;/h2&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;span class=&quot;flshead&quot;&gt; &lt;i&gt;Date published: &lt;b&gt;3/17/2010&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/i&gt; &lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;&lt;/style&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;BY KEITH EPPS&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p/&gt; &lt;p&gt;A local man suspected of multiple burglaries over the weekend was arrested Monday after his image was captured on a surveillance camera, police said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Charles Pace, 23, who has no fixed address, was charged with 16 offenses, including multiple counts of burglary and grand larceny.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;According to Fredericksburg police spokeswoman Natatia Bledsoe, Pace is accused of breaking into six city businesses over the weekend.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;All of the businesses--Merryman&#39;s Service Center, Pulliam&#39;s Auto, Kenmore Cleaners, JT Automotive, Graves Auto Service and Battlefield Motorcycles--are in the same general area of the city.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The burglar stole cash in amounts from $50 to nearly $1,000 from five of the businesses. Laptop computers, a cash register and a flashlight were also taken.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;City detectives were investigating the thefts Monday when they found that the surveillance camera at Battlefield Motorcycles on Lafayette Boulevard had gotten a picture of the suspect.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;SUSPECT SPOTTED BY OFFICER IN PARKING LOT&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Police recognized Pace on the picture, and a detective spotted him a short time later walking through a commuter lot downtown.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;He was taken into custody without incident and placed in the Rappahannock Regional Jail under no bond. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Bledsoe said Pace was cooperative with police after his arrest.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Pace was also charged with destruction of property and carrying a concealed weapon. He had a pellet gun on him when he was arrested, Bledsoe said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;View the Stafford County community page&quot;&gt;Stafford County&lt;/a&gt; authorities are also investigating Pace in connection with thefts there, police said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Keith Epps: 540/374-5404&lt;br/&gt; Email: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:kepps@freelancestar.com&quot;&gt;kepps@freelancestar.com&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;br/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.addthis.com/bookmark.php&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://s9.addthis.com/button1-share.gif&quot; width=&quot;125&quot; height=&quot;16&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; alt=&quot;&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;p&gt;  Read more stories about &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;Fredericksburg&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;flshead&quot;&gt; &lt;i&gt;Date published: &lt;b&gt;3/17/2010&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/i&gt; &lt;/span&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;    &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;  &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;  &lt;br/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;&lt;/style&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;  &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. In a &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-cM9S2AzU28&quot;&gt;YouTube posting, &lt;/a&gt;the vehicle pulls off what BMW calls &quot;the oldest trick in the world&quot;: the bike snatches a tablecloth out from under a full banquet setting, without upsetting anything.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;That simple idea, along with a soundtrack mixing rock, classical music, and a roaring engine, has gotten BMW more than 1.4 million clicks and an online advertising award earlier this month, the company said. (The incredible video is loud, but otherwise suitable for work.)&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://i.bnet.com/blogs/bmwtable.jpg&quot;&gt;&lt;img class=&quot;alignleft size-full wp-image-4112&quot; title=&quot;bmwtable, BMW, motorcyle&quot; src=&quot;http://i.bnet.com/blogs/bmwtable.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; width=&quot;120&quot; height=&quot;90&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;In the Venn diagram of the &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://industry.bnet.com/auto/10001736/bmw-wins-two-effies-iffier-effies-for-nissan-carscom/&quot;&gt;BMW brand image&lt;/a&gt;, there&#39;s not much overlap between motorcycles and cars. In fact, for most people there&#39;s no overlap, because they&#39;re not even aware the company makes motorcycles. That&#39;s frustrating to BMW, because its automotive employees are proud of the bikes, too, and many of its highest-ranking auto executives are also motorcycle enthusiasts&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Both kinds of BMW have a lot in common: high-performance technology, a reputation for being among the best-in-class; and a &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://industry.bnet.com/auto/1000199/bmw-ends-16-year-streak-of-ever-higher-sales/&quot;&gt;high price tag&lt;/a&gt;. In relative terms, BMW motorcycles may be even more expensive, exclusive and high-performance than the automobiles. For instance, the BMW S 1000 RR goes from zero to 62 mph in only 2.9 seconds, much faster than any ordinary car. This is what allows it to pull off the tablecloth trick.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Maybe this video, which doesn&#39;t mention cars, will get BMW motorcycles the attention the company craves.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Photo: YouTube via BMW&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.examiner.com/x-38265-Detroit-Automotive-Examiner~y2010m3d13-Review-2010-Suzuki-Kizashi-SLS-great-chassis-in-need-of-a-better-drivetrain&quot;&gt;Review: 2010 Suzuki Kizashi SLS, great chassis in need ... - Examiner&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 13 Mar 2010 08:01 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;examiners_body&quot;&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13;&lt;div&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13;&lt;/div&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;div class=&quot;iconpanel&quot;&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/icon/tinytweets.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww%2Eexaminer%2Ecom%2Fx%2D38265%2DDetroit%2DAutomotive%2DExaminer%7Ey2010m3d13%2DReview%2D2010%2DSuzuki%2DKizashi%2DSLS%2Dgreat%2Dchassis%2Din%2Dneed%2Dof%2Da%2Dbetter%2Ddrivetrain&quot;&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/icon/tinyfb.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;ovalbutton&quot; title=&quot;comments&quot;&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;span&gt;&amp;#13; Comment&amp;#13; &amp;#13;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#13; &amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Print this page&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/icon/printer.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Email this page&quot; id=&quot;emailshow&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/email.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#13;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://rss.examiner.com/RSS-38265-Detroit-Automotive-Examiner.rss&quot; title=&quot;RSS Feed&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/icon/feed.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#13; &lt;span&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; id=&quot;subscribeshow&quot; class=&quot; ovalbutton&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://image.examiner.com/img/icon/subscribe.gif&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; align=&quot;left&quot;/&gt; Subscribe&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;div id=&quot;subscribecontent&quot; class=&quot;hide&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;h2&gt;Subscribe&lt;/h2&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;myformgoeshere&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/span&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt; &amp;#13;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;387&quot; width=&quot;580&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_580_1.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Picture if you will a handsome looking four door sedan, sized on the smaller end of the mid-size market. It has a nicely styled and appointed interior. Power from the four cylinder engine is put to the road through an advanced all-wheel-drive system. This car can handle curvy rural roads with the grace you&#39;d expect of a car developed on German autobahns and racetracks. This description sounds an awful light like an &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.google.com/url?sa=t&amp;amp;source=web&amp;amp;ct=res&amp;amp;cd=1&amp;amp;ved=0CAsQFjAA&amp;amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.greenfuelsforecast.com%2FDisplayNewsroom.php%3FnewsroomID%3D1&amp;amp;ei=_p2bS9G-MJDuM4egueYN&amp;amp;usg=AFQjCNHQMlyIiFxv4aFijjxorY54TImsFg&amp;amp;sig2=tB2W4SaFxumW4Yznqf2XBg&quot;&gt;Audi A4&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;387&quot; width=&quot;580&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_580_3.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In fact we just spent a week with the new Suzuki Kizashi. When people hear the name Suzuki, they generally think either small SUVs or motorcycles, often very, very fast motorcycles. Cars not so much. The Kizashi is Suzuki&#39;s latest attempt to break into the heart of the U.S. car market. Suzuki is one of the best selling car brands in Japan but it does so selling tiny urban commuters for the crowded streets of cities like Tokyo and Osaka. Americans prefer something more ample in size. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Kizashi first appeared as a series of concepts that grabbed a lot of attention in 2007 and 2008. The design was toned significantly by the time it hit the streets of America in late 2009 but this is still a good looking car. At 183.1 long overall, the Kizashi is 7 inches shorter than a Ford Fusion and the wheelbase is 1.1 inches less than the Ford. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The pronounced shoulder curve that runs the length of the body combines with the flared wheel arches and relatively short overhangs to give the Kizashi an athletic looking stance. The standard 18 inch alloy wheels on our SLS test example add to that planted, hunkered down appearance avoiding the small wheel, tippy look of some past Suzuki cars. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;At the front the tall, bold grille looks almost Audi-esque giving the impression that this upstart really does want to challenge the respected German. Move inside the Kizashi and the upscale impression continues. Even though the dash is predominantly composed of hard rather than soft-touch plastics, it looks good. The seats are covered in black leather as are the thick rimmed steering wheel and part of the door panels above the arm rest. The front seats are comfortable and offer decent amount of lateral support for more spirited driving. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Kizashi SLS that we drove was equipped with a 425 watt Rockford-Fosgate audio system with 10 speakers. The audio system sounds good with all kinds of music. All Kizashis get a USB port to connect an iPod. Unfortunately the controls on the audio system only allow forward and back control through the current playlist. navigating the entire menu doesn&#39;t seem to be possible. &lt;br /&gt;Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;187&quot; width=&quot;280&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_280_1.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;187&quot; width=&quot;280&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_280_2.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;All Kizashis from the base $18,999 S model up to the top SLS trim level get automatic dual zone climate control with additional vents at back end of the center console. The back seat isn&#39;t as roomy as what you&#39;ll find in a larger Toyota Camry or Honda Accord. It will however accommodate a 6 foot 14 year old in reasonable comfort. As with most cars in this segment, three adults will find themselves rather crowded in back, but kids shouldn&#39;t have any problem.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;187&quot; width=&quot;280&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_280_3.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;187&quot; width=&quot;280&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_280_4.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For now all Kizashis are powered by a 2.4-liter inline-four that produces 185 horsepower with the six-speed manual transmission or 180 hp with the optional continuously variable transmission (CVT). CVT equipped cars like our tester get paddle shifters on the back of the steering wheel allowing some limited degree of manual control. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;CVTs have generally not found favor with most American drivers because of the way that they allow the engine to rev up to some fixed speed and hold it there as the car accelerates and drive ratio changes. In the case of the Kizashi, that generally means the engine spins up to about 4,000 rpm and holds there. Some other CVT equipped sport sedans are programmed to operate across a set of fixed ratios more like a conventional automatic transmission. The CVT in the Kizashi also seems to sap much of the life out of the engine, leaving the car feeling sluggish even when shifting manually. We&#39;d recommend that those looking for more fun stick with the manual transmission.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;387&quot; width=&quot;580&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_580_2.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The highlight of the Kizashi comes on the open road. Suzuki spent a significant amount of its development time tuning the suspension at the legendary Nurburgring race track in Germany. The Kizashi has excellent body control just the right balance of spring rates and damping. The roads around our part of southeast Michigan are notoriously bad but the Kizashi remains on an even keel at all times. The suspension absorbs the frost heaves and potholes very well for a car with such large wheels and low profile tires.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Around corners the steering is direct and precise although feedback could be better. The all wheel drive provided sure-footed grip during some late winter snow, making this a viable alternative to a Subaru Legacy or a Quattro equipped Audi A4.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;387&quot; width=&quot;580&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_580_4.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The CVT is not particularly responsive to commands issued with the paddle shifters. Ratio changes are lethargic and the ratios you get aren&#39;t always predictable. Instead of gears 2,3,4 and 5 always being the same, the transmission control seems to modify them based on the conditions. For what is billed as a sports sedan by Suzuki, the transmission control should be more predictable. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Aside from the unimpressive CVT, the Kizashi is a pleasantly compact, nimble and agile drivers car. Later this year Suzuki is expected to add a V6 engine to the lineup and a hybrid powertrain is under development. Personally we&#39;d like to see Suzuki skip the V6 and go with a turbocharged version of the four. Pair that with a dual clutch transmission like Volkswagen&#39;s DSG and you&#39;d have a powertrain capable of taking advantage of this chassis making it a true cut-rate Audi. It would likely do better than the 22 mpg we saw in a week of driving the CVT car.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img height=&quot;387&quot; width=&quot;580&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://image3.examiner.com/images/blog/EXID38265/images/kazashi_580_5.jpg&quot;/&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Â &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Kizashi starts at $18,999 for a front wheel drive S model with manual transmission. Our thoroughly equipped SLS with all wheel drive had a bottom line of $27,484 including delivery charges.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://thm-a01.yimg.com/nimage/79570e3546d4573a&quot; alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;This posting includes an audio/video/photo media file: &lt;a href=&quot;http://img.turbo.fr/02332544-photo-suzuki-kizashi.jpg&quot;&gt;Download Now&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://blog.seattlepi.nwsource.com/seattle911/archives/148993.asp&quot;&gt;Are loud motorcycles legal? - Seattle Post Intelligencer&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 08 Mar 2010 08:18 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;blogentrytext&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;Different forms of this question came from several readers: &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;b&gt;Q:&lt;/b&gt; Are motorcycles with loud exhausts legal? Do they ever get ticketed?&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;b&gt;A:&lt;/b&gt; Police say some motorcycle exhaust systems are illegal, though specific statistics on how often Seattle motorcycle riders get cited for them were not available.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Seattle Police spokesman Mark Jamieson references Seattle Municipal Code 11.57.280:&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;blockquote&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;No person shall modify the exhaust system of a motorcycle in a manner which will amplify or increase the noise emitted by the engine of such vehicle above that emitted by the muffler originally installed on the vehicle, and it shall be unlawful for any person to operate a motorcycle not equipped as required by Sections 11.84.060 and 11.84.080 or which has been amplified as prohibited by this section so that the vehicle&#39;s exhaust noise exceeds ninety-five (95) decibels as measured by the Society of Automotive Engineers (SAE) test procedure J1169, (May, 1998). (RCW 46.37.390(3))&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;/blockquote&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;It doesn&#39;t have to be modified,&quot; Jamieson said of a motorcycle&#39;s exhaust system. &quot;If someone is sitting there with a stock motorcycle and its really loud, they would be cited for excessive noise.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;People on bikes violating the city law can get a $124 ticket. But how often are those tickets issued?&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;It really depends on how busy the night is,&quot; he said. &quot;If there are shootings and robberies and assaults, we&#39;re not going to be citing people for excessive noise on vehicles because we&#39;re too busy.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Calls to police are prioritized depending on the severity of the call. But police say all 911 calls get some kind of response.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;According to section 11.84.080 of the &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://clerk.ci.seattle.wa.us/~scripts/nph-brs.exe?s1=11.84.080&amp;amp;s2=&amp;amp;S3=&amp;amp;Sect4=AND&amp;amp;l=20&amp;amp;Sect3=PLURON&amp;amp;Sect5=CODE1&amp;amp;d=CODE&amp;amp;p=1&amp;amp;u=%2F%7Epublic%2Fcode1.htm&amp;amp;r=1&amp;amp;Sect6=HITOFF&amp;amp;f=G&quot;&gt;code&lt;/a&gt;, all motor vehicles must be equipped with a muffler in good working order at all times and in constant operation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; A quiet library averages 30 decibels; a lawnmower averages 90 decibels, according to the American Speech-Language-Hearing Association. An alarm clock or busy street average 80 decibels; a jet engine and firearms average 130 decibels, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.asha.org/public/hearing/disorders/noise.htm&quot;&gt;according to the Association&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Jim McCaslin, president and chief operating officer of Harley-Davidson Motor Company, called the issue of excessive motorcycle noise one of the company&#39;s toughest challenges &quot;because of its potential to divide and destroy our sport.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Here&#39;s &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.harley-davidson.com/wcm/Content/Pages/2006_Campaigns/noise_popup.jsp?locale=en_US&quot;&gt;more&lt;/a&gt; of McCaslin&#39;s comments from the Harley-Davidson Web site:&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;blockquote&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Today, Harley-Davidson motorcycles have more power and performance than our predecessors could have ever imagined, but with all due respect, we love to hear them coming. That doesn&#39;t mean louder noise equals even more power, however. It&#39;s an interesting misconception. Testing has proven that straight pipes do not necessarily outperform pipes with lower noise levels. Pick the wrong pipes and you can severely reduce your horsepower and/or your torque. And while you&#39;re doing it, you&#39;ll awaken the sleeping giant of social concern that lives next door to all of us.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;/blockquote&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Thanks to people who submitted questions. &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:caseymcnerthney@seattlepi.com&quot;&gt;Please keep submitting questions&lt;/a&gt;. Who is at fault?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://blog.seattlepi.nwsource.com/seattle911/archives/147707.asp&quot;&gt;Do you have to drive all the way around traffic circles?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; href=&quot;http://blog.seattlepi.nwsource.com/seattle911/archives/144581.asp&quot;&gt;Why don&#39;t police arrest more Critical Mass cyclists?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://blog.seattlepi.nwsource.com/seattle911/archives/143736.asp&quot;&gt;When do school speed zone limits apply?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Datamonitor&#39;s Automotive: Poland Industry Guide is an essential resource for top-level data and analysis covering the Poland Automotive industry. It includes detailed data on market size and segmentation, textual analysis of the key trends and competitive landscape, and profiles of the leading companies. This incisive report provides expert analysis with distinct chapters for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, &lt;/p&gt; New Cars and Trucks&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Scope of the Report&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; * Contains an executive summary and data on value, volume and segmentation for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, New Cars and Trucks&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * Provides textual analysis of the industry&#39;s prospects, competitive landscape and profiles of the leading companies&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * Incorporates in-depth five forces competitive environment analysis and scorecards&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * Includes five-year forecasts for Light trucks, Medium &amp;amp; Heavy Trucks, Motorcycles, New Cars and Trucks&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Highlights&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; * The Polish trucks market generated total revenues of $2.9 billion in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -1% for the period spanning 2005-2009.&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * The Polish light trucks market generated total revenues of $831.1 million in 2009, representing a compound annual growth rate (CAGR) of 3.6% for the period spanning 2005-2009.&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * The Polish medium and heavy trucks market generated total revenues of $2.1 billion in 2009, representing a compound annual rate of change (CARC) of -2.6% for the period spanning 2005-2009.&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * The Polish motorcycles market generated total revenues of $379.2 million in 2008, representing a compound annual growth rate (CAGR) of 75.7% for the period spanning 2004-2008.&lt;br /&gt;&amp;#13; * The Polish new cars market generated total revenues of $7 billion in 2009, representing a compound annual growth rate (CAGR) of 5.9% for the period spanning 2005-2009.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Johnson Controls (NYSE: JCI - News) is the global leader that brings ingenuity to the places where people live, work and travel. By integrating technologies, products and services, we create smart environments that redefine the relationships between people and their surroundings. Our team of 140,000 employees creates a more comfortable, safe and sustainable world through our products and services for more than 200 million vehicles, 12 million homes and one million commercial buildings. Our commitment to sustainability drives our environmental stewardship, good corporate citizenship in our workplaces and communities, and the products and services we provide to customers. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.orlandosentinel.com/business/os-auto-scscolumn-031410-20100313,0,7602064.story&quot;&gt;Steven Cole Smith, Orlando Sentinel Automotive Editor - Orlando Sentinel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 12 Mar 2010 06:22 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;story-body-text&quot;&gt;In 1996, Bill Warner, a Jacksonville businessman and car collector, decided to put on a car show, so he and his friends assembled some nice vehicles, drawing a modest crowd of 2,200 and raising some money for charity.&lt;p&gt; To say the Amelia Island Concours has grown is an understatement. &quot;This show is as good as it gets,&quot; says Keith Canouse, an Orlando car collector. &quot;I think it&#39;s the best in the country,&quot; perhaps even surpassing the Pebble Beach Concours, regarded as the king of all car shows, held each year since 1950 in California. Canouse is part of a contingent from the Orlando area that is displaying at Amelia this weekend â he&#39;s bringing his 1914 Renault.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;Amelia is a user-friendly show,&quot; Canouse says. Warner goes out of his way to make everyone feel welcome, not just the automotive elite. One reason: Warner and his co-chariman, Tom Cotter, consider themselves just a couple of car guys. Cotter has an important collection of Shelby Cobras and Shelby Ford Mustangs, but his daily drive is a 2004 Mini Cooper.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Given the fact that the show, this weekend celebrating its 15th anniversary on Amelia Island near Jacksonville, is considered on par with Pebble Beach, celebrating its 60th birthday this summer, speaks to the work Warner has done. &quot;It doesn&#39;t get easier,&quot; Warner says. &quot;Every year has its own set of problems.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Such as: Warner, a motorsports enthusiast, always packs the four-day program with multiple racing seminars that draw fans who may or may not be interested in classic cars. This year, he assembled a trio of race drivers unparallel in their influence: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;taxInlineTagLink&quot; title=&quot;Richard Petty&quot; id=&quot;PESPT008516&quot;&gt;Richard Petty&lt;/a&gt;, 72, the winningest &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;taxInlineTagLink&quot; title=&quot;NASCAR&quot; id=&quot;15039007&quot;&gt;NASCAR&lt;/a&gt; driver ever; Don Garlits, 78, considered the king of drag racing, and Sir Stirling Moss, who competed from 1948 to 1962, winning an incredible 212 of the 529 races he entered, including 16 Formula 1 races.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; But last week, Moss, 80, fell at his home in England, breaking both ankles and multiple other bones. Warner&#39;s legendary trio became a duo until another legend, racer and car builder Carroll Shelby, agreed to step in. That Shelby, 87 and with a transplanted heart and kidney, would drop everything and come to Florida on such short notice speaks to the influence of Amelia and Bill Warner.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Sunday, the show will draw more than 10,000 people for the judging of the 250-plus vehicles on display, chosen from thousands entered. It&#39;s an invitation-only show, and just being accepted to display at Amelia, much less win your class, adds to a vehicle&#39;s cachet and value.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Among those displaying is Dave Brewer of Longwood, bringing his 1953 Buick Skylark hardtop. It is one of a kind â &quot;It&#39;s entered in a class called, &#39;Cars you never even realized were built,&#39;&quot; Brewer says. Buick built some Skylark convertibles, but the company built one hardtop just to gauge the reaction. &quot;Usually, cars like that were destroyed after they were shown, but this one survived,&quot; he says, because the wife of a &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;taxInlineTagLink&quot; title=&quot;General Motors Corp.&quot; id=&quot;ORCRP006407&quot;&gt;General Motors&lt;/a&gt; executive liked the car, and it was customized for her tastes. &quot;Amelia Island is the kind of show you just can&#39;t miss,&quot; Brewer says. &quot;The quality of cars is amazing.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; And it isn&#39;t just cars: Each year, Warner selects a few brands to feature, and this year, one of them is Triumph motorcycles. Mike Crone of &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;taxInlineTagLink&quot; title=&quot;Mount Dora&quot; id=&quot;PLGEO100100405050000&quot;&gt;Mount Dora&lt;/a&gt; has a national reputation as a Triumph restorer and collector, and he&#39;s bringing four bikes: A 1950, 1951 and 1953 model, plus his favorite: &quot;A 1938 Triumph, an original Speed Twin formerly owned by Bud Ekins,&quot; a late and legendary stuntman who was the riding partner of actor &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; class=&quot;taxInlineTagLink&quot; title=&quot;Steve McQueen&quot; id=&quot;PECLB003194&quot;&gt;Steve McQueen&lt;/a&gt;. Crone has never even been to the Amelia Island show, but he&#39;s aware of the reputation. &quot;I&#39;m looking forward to being a part of it,&quot; he says.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Each year, the Amelia Island Concours raises more than $100,000 for charities that include the Community Hospice of Northeast Florida and the Spina Bifida Association. The show begins at 9:30 a.m. and ends at 5 p.m. Sunday, with judging beginning at 11 a.m. Admission is $50 for adults, $20 for ages 12-18, and free for ages 11 and under.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; For more information, including how to get there on the grounds of the Ritz-Carlton Hotel on Amelia Island, log onto AmeliaConcours.org&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Sentinel Automotive Editor Steven Cole Smith can be reached at &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:scsmith@orlandosentinel.com&quot;&gt;scsmith@orlandosentinel.com&lt;/a&gt;  &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.newssun.com/sports/FRI-3-12-STARS&quot;&gt;Special STARS Softball Classic continues to grow - News-Sun&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 12 Mar 2010 05:00 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;mosContainerPadding&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;published: Friday, March 12, 2010&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.addthis.com/bookmark.php?v=20&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://s7.addthis.com/static/btn/lg-addthis-en.gif&quot; width=&quot;125&quot; height=&quot;16&quot; alt=&quot;Bookmark and Share&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;h3&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;Special STARS Softball Classic continues to grow&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Special to the News-Sun&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;SEBRING - The Special STARS Softball Classic grows every year with more and more local athletes showing an interest in playing ball with individuals with disabilities.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The roster for this year&#39;s 11th annual event increased by adding one more team that will play in the tournament on Saturday, March 13, at the Highlands County Sports Complex. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;There have been seven local teams practicing for the past three weeks to go up against two teams from Fort Lauderdale.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The newest addition to this year&#39;s list of teams is the Avon Park Youth Academy headed up by coach Pete Zeegers.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Other team sponsors are Coffee News, coached by Andy Basso; Beef O&#39;Brady&#39;s led by Amy Torres; Florida Hospital Heartland Division, coached by Craig Couch; McPhail&#39;s Auto Sales, led by Bobby Sexton; Duffer&#39;s Sports Grille, coached by David Sipos; and Dee&#39;s Place, led by Tim Ritenour.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The main All-Star sponsors for the entire tournament are Highlands Sertoma Club and Wal-Mart of Avon Park and Sebring. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The Sebring Elks Lodge 1529 is sponsoring the shirts for the volunteers. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;All of these sponsors will have representatives present to toss out the first pitch of the tournament.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;For special athletes wishing to learn the skills of playing softball, there is a skill level sponsored by Aaction Pest Control and Lampe &amp;amp; Kiefer Hearing Aid Center. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;These individuals have been practicing four different skills and will compete for ribbons on Saturday. They will be tested on throwing, fielding, batting and running the bases.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Playing action begins at 8 a.m. with an opening ceremony at 7:45 a.m. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The Heartland Riders Association will carry in the American flag by motorcycle followed by the national anthem. The Heartland Riders are also sponsoring part of the lunch for the athletes and will be on hand to distribute it. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Athletes with disabilities have been evenly distributed to each team. The slow-pitch softball game has four special athletes playing with three male and three female partners in the community.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The public is invited to come and cheer on the local teams. There will be a concession stand selling hot dogs, french fries, chips and sodas to benefit Special STARS.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;There will be a Home Run Derby open to anyone. It will be $5 for 10 balls and the winner will get half of the money raised in their division while the other half goes to Special STARS. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Each batter selects their own pitcher and there will be three different levels - men, women and special athletes.&amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Other tournament sponsors include Doris and David Magowan, Morris Funeral Chapel, Heacock Insurance Agency, Reflections on Silver Lake, Highlands Independent Bank, Beta Sigma Phi, Stephenson-Nelson Funeral Home, Roadhouse Grill, King Equipment, Frames &amp;amp; Images, Donna Lyles and Anissa Jones, and Jim and Carol Phipps. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;The Highlands County Board of County Commissioners allow Special STARS to use the fields at no cost.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 12 Mar 2010 05:00 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;content&quot;&gt;&lt;dl id=&quot;contactInfo&quot;&gt;&lt;dt&gt;Contact Information&lt;/dt&gt; &lt;dd class=&quot;contactName&quot;&gt;Louis Bledsoe&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;Owner&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;MotorNetExpress.com&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;505-688-4410&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:sales@betrmpg.com&quot;&gt;sales@betrmpg.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;/dl&gt;&lt;p&gt;Albuquerque, New Mexico&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Enerpulse, Inc., manufacturer of Pulstar Pulse Plugs, has begun shipping their new Platinum and Iridium Pulstars to resellers.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Previewed to the automotive aftermarket community at the SEMA show in Las Vegas this past November, the new Pulstars bring the durability of noble metal electrodes to the revolutionary technology of the Pulstar Pulse Plug.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Increasing consumer demand and the establishment of distribution through several national auto parts stores has brought the company to new production levels, resulting in new efficiencies and cost savings in the manufacturing process. The original copper electrode Pulstar sold for $24.95 (or more) per plug during most of first year and a half of production, and recently became available at an MSRP of $12.95 as new &#39;Generation 3&#39; manufacturing technology was fully implemented.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&quot;Pulstars are much more complex internally than spark plugs, but they must be exactly the same size externally, so we have always been challenged with physical durability, particularly of the porcelain component. With Generation 3, our failure rate is consistent with other high quality spark plugs on the market.&quot; reports Lou Camilli, President and Chief Technical Officer of Enerpulse. &quot;Now, as we introduce the Platinum and Iridium electrode models, we offer additional choice to the consumer, based on their driving style. The Platinum Pulstar is a significant upgrade from the earlier copper electrode Pulstars, but we are suggesting a retail price of only $9.95 per plug, a 20% cost reduction simultaneous with a major increase in service life due to the extra durability of platinum vs. copper.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Driving styles fall into two broad categories, according to extensive market research. &quot;Just as many people consider fuel economy very strongly in their vehicle purchase decisions, many also DRIVE their vehicles with a deliberate effort to conserve gas. They are gentle on the accelerator, they don&#39;t have to be in the fast lane to be comfortable, and they keep their air filter and oil changes on schedule. These drivers will upgrade to Platinum Pulstar Plugs and see an improvement in fuel economy of 7%, or more. This translates to recovering the cost of a set of brand new Pulstar Platinum plugs in about ten thousand miles of driving a six cylinder sedan and paying $2.50 a gallon for gas. Higher gas prices mean an even faster payback.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The other category of drivers uses the accelerator a bit like an adrenalin pump. We all have our moments. Acceleration just feels good; maybe it&#39;s a control thing. And the largest sporting events in the world are conducted at race tracks. &quot;At $12.95 each, Iridium Pulstar Plugs provide a much lower &#39;cost per horsepower gained&#39; than aftermarket mods such as air intake or exhaust systems. We have seen as much as a 17% increase in some vehicles, but 2% to 3% is more realistic. The 2% to 3% in TORQUE that is also typically achieved is the real attention getter.&quot; Drivers consistently report a different &quot;feel&quot;, especially when just beginning to accelerate. &quot;TORQUE is what you FEEL!&quot; It was obvious that Camilli identifies with category B.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Enerpulse is also introducing the Iridium Pulstar in two sizes that will fit over 1,800 popular motorcycles, including Harley Davidson, Honda, Yamaha, and BMW models. &quot;Motorcycle riders are much more sensitive to performance, and we have gotten an extremely enthusiastic reaction from the riding community!&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;One of Pulstars&#39; most ardent resellers is Lou Bledsoe, who markets Pulstars on eBay and his own website. &quot;100% positive feedback and almost every transaction has been a Pulstar sale.&quot; Bledsoe is a classic Category A driver. He has been using Pulstars in his family vehicles since hearing about them on NPR in April of 2008. &quot;We installed the Pulstars in a Volvo, a BMW, and our faithful 1997 Jeep Grand Cherokee 4Ã4 V8 with over 150,000 miles on it. They all improved, but the Jeep amazed us, jumping up to over 19 miles per gallon on the highway.&quot; If you have to be convinced to be convincing, both Lou&#39;s will look you in the eye without blinking. &quot;Pulstar Pulse Plugs make a difference you can feel as you drive, a difference you can measure with a dynamometer and emissions tester, and a difference you can count in dollars and cents at the gas pump.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p id=&quot;wwguid&quot;&gt;WebWireID114083&lt;/p&gt; &lt;dl id=&quot;relatedLinks&quot;&gt;&lt;dt&gt;Related Links&lt;/dt&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.pulstarpulseplugs.info&quot;&gt;Learn more about Pulstar Pulse Plugs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://stores.ebay.com/BetrMPG-Pulstar-Plug-Specialist&quot;&gt;Buy Pulstar Pulse Spark Plugs on eBay&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;/dl&gt;&lt;dl id=&quot;relatedKeywords&quot;&gt;&lt;dt&gt;Â &lt;/dt&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot; &quot;/&gt;Pulstar Spark Plugs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot; &quot;/&gt;Pulstar Pulse Plugs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot; &quot;/&gt;Pulstar Plugs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot; &quot;/&gt;Best Spark Plugs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;dd&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot; &quot;/&gt;Iridium Platinum Pulstar&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/dd&gt; &lt;/dl&gt;&lt;p class=&quot;newsDisclaimer&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This news content may be integrated into any legitimate news gathering and publishing effort. &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div&gt;Sorry, readability was unable to parse this page for content.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.nbc15.com/home/headlines/87344767.html&quot;&gt;CrimeTracker 15: Burglary Suspects Arrested - nbc15.com&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 11 Mar 2010 08:07 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;headlines&quot; id=&quot;storyText&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Posted Thursday, March 11, 2010 --- 10:10 a.m.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Press Release from the Rock County Sheriff&#39;s Office:&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;On March 9, 2010, Detectives from the Rock County Sheriff&#39;s Office, along with Deputies from the Rock County Special Investigations Unit, served search warrants at 424 and 426 Center Avenue in the City of Janesville. Detectives were looking for stolen property that was being kept in these residences. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Detectives had been investigating burglaries to storage facilities since November 2009. The storage facilities were located in townships outside the City of Janesville. Individual storage units were being burglarized at numerous storage facilities. Items that were being stolen during the burglaries ranged from tools, luggage, vehicle wheels, automotive racing parts, motorcycles and snowmobiles.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;During the investigation, Detectives developed suspects in these burglaries. The investigation culminated on March 9 when Detectives were able to recover a significant amount of stolen property. The property was recovered during consent searches and during two search warrants. Over $40,000 worth of property was recovered. Property was also recovered from burglaries that occurred in the City of Janesville and Beloit Township. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Recovered items include: A snowmobile, a motorcycle, high performance racing parts, a flat screen TV, luggage, tools, collectible coins, a go-kart, several sets of vehicle wheels, golf clubs, and an assortment of other items. These items will be returned to their respective owners. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;At this point in the investigation, four subjects were arrested as a result of this investigation. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;They are:&lt;br/&gt;Zachary L. Trezek, 18 years of age&lt;br/&gt;Adam J. Hollis, 17 years of age&lt;br/&gt;426 Center Avenue&lt;br/&gt;Janesville, WI 53545&lt;br/&gt;Charge: Burglary and Theft&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Gregory C. Lehr, 18 years of age&lt;br/&gt;109 North Atwood Avenue&lt;br/&gt;Janesville, WI 53545&lt;br/&gt;Charge: Burglary and Theft&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Dylan R. Lambert, 18 years of age&lt;br/&gt;201 North Grant&lt;br/&gt;Janesville, WI 53545&lt;br/&gt;Charge: Burglary and Theft&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;All four subjects were initially arrested on one charge of burglary and theft each. The investigation is continuing and it is anticipated that more counts of burglary and theft will be referred to the District Attorney&#39;s Office on all four subjects.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Initial Appearance: Monday, April 12, 2010, at 1:00PM.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Pursuant to the directive of the Wisconsin Supreme Court, as found in Supreme Court Rule 20:3.6, Trial Publicity, you are advised that a charge is merely an accusation and that a defendant is presumed innocent until proven guilty.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.theautochannel.com/F/news/2010/03/11/468810.html&quot;&gt;Winningest Female In Professional Motorsports History ... - The Auto Chanel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 11 Mar 2010 08:00 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;article-text&quot;&gt;&lt;br clear=&quot;all&quot;/&gt;&lt;p&gt;NEW ORLEANS, March 11, 2010: Angelle Sampey, who is the winningest female in professional motorsports history, is hanging up her helmet and leathers as she announces her retirement as a professional drag racer. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Sampey, who totaled 41 victories during a 13-year NHRA Pro Stock Motorcycle career, said she&#39;s planning to pursue other career opportunities while looking to start a family with her fiancÃ©, Seth Drago. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;I&#39;m ready for a new challenge, including opening Coral Fever, a store specializing in fish, coral and aquariums,&quot; said the 39-year-old. &quot;I made the ultimate sacrifice to postpone starting a family when I began racing. Now, I&#39;m going to make the ultimate sacrifice to stop racing to get married (in June) and then try and start a family.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The Louisiana native made her NHRA debut in 1996 at Bandimere Speedway outside of Denver and immediately raised eyebrows by advancing to the semifinals. She recorded her first win in her first final round later that season at Reading, Pa. in the fourth event of her career. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;I will take away so many great memories from racing,&quot; she said. &quot;I&#39;m certainly going to miss being around my fellow racers and, of course, the fans. I really enjoyed meeting the fans at every race. They were always there for me through the good times and the bad times.&quot; To be sure, Sampey did not experience many bad times since &#39;96. In fact, she captured three world championships and banked 18 wins between 2000 and 2002. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;Obviously, that was an extraordinarily exciting time period,&quot; she offered. &quot;I never imagined I could have that kind of success. I was very fortunate to be surrounded by a lot of talented people including George Bryce (her crew chief during each championship season).&quot; It was in 2001 when Sampey became the winningest female in NHRA history, moving past Shirley Muldowney on the list. She went on to pocket seven wins that season which remains the most wins ever recorded in a single season by a female competitor in NHRA history. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;To be honest, it was tough to comprehend what I had done after I surpassed Shirley&#39;s win total (18),&quot; she said. &quot;After all, Shirley is one of the sport&#39;s legends. I look up to her.&quot; Among Sampey&#39;s final stats will be a staggering 364 round wins out of 506 total rounds of competition or a win roughly 72 percent of the time she blasted down the quarter-mile. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;Again, I want to emphasize that I had a bunch of people help me along the way,&quot; she related. &quot;I could spend a day or more thanking each and every one. I&#39;ll never forget any of them.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Perhaps, the one mark Sampey wishes she could have broken before exiting the sport was the most wins in the Pro Stock Motorcycle class â 45 â as established by the late Dave Schultz. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &quot;That&#39;s probably true,&quot; she said. &quot;I clearly could&#39;ve hung around just to try and break that record. But, as I stated, it&#39;s time for a change.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;4&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.newsok.com/its-no-mystery-that-writing-is-oklahoma-womans-passion/article/3445329?custom_click=pod_headline_ae&quot;&gt;It&amp;rsquo;s no mystery that writing is Oklahoma woman&amp;rsquo;s ... - Daily Oklahoman&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 11 Mar 2010 06:06 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;articleBody hnews hentry item&quot;&gt;  &lt;span&gt;Â©2009 Produced by NewsOK.com. All rights reserved.&lt;/span&gt; &lt;img src=&quot;http://analytics.apnewsregistry.com/analytics/Image.svc/Oklahoman/3445329/Env/prod&quot; height=&quot;1&quot; width=&quot;1&quot; alt=&quot;&quot;/&gt; &lt;br/&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;entry-content&quot;&gt; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Mary Cash&quot;&gt;Mary Cash&lt;/a&gt; leaned over a hospital bed to hear what she thought were her mother&#39;s last words. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;ad300&quot;&gt; &lt;span class=&quot;hmedia&quot;&gt; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://s3.amazonaws.com/newsok-photos/878750/medium.jpg&quot; class=&quot;thickbox&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://photos.newsok.com/2/showimage/878750/medium&quot; width=&quot;300&quot;/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;br/&gt;&lt;h3 class=&quot;bar color&quot;&gt;Multimedia&lt;/h3&gt; &lt;h3 class=&quot;color bar&quot;&gt;More Info&lt;/h3&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;container top&quot;&gt; &lt;b&gt; Books written by Mary Ellen Cooper&lt;/b&gt;&lt;p&gt;â¢ &quot;Unlikely Assassins&quot; (1992).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Blood and Pity&quot; (1994).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Murder at the Locksmith Convention&quot; (1997). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;The Wright Special&quot; (1998). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Fatal Trust&quot; (2000). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Key Deceptions&quot; (2000). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Uncivil Death&quot; (2001). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Key Confrontations&quot; (2003).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Slow Death ... and Other Oklahoma Murders&quot; (June 2003). &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Uncivil Death in Norfolk&quot; (2004).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Deadly Patterns&quot; (2004).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Deadly Redlands&quot; (2004).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Murder in Mexico&quot; (2005).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Bold and Brassy&quot; (2007).&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; Cooper wrote short stories included in these anthologies:&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Almostly Murder ... With Pets&quot; in 2002.&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;â¢ &quot;Remindful Murder With Colorful Kin&quot; in 2008.&lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p/&gt;&amp;#13; She also compiled a cookbook titled &quot;In the Kitchen with Oklahoma First Ladies 1907-1957,&quot; published in 2008. &lt;p/&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;span class=&quot;entry-content&quot;&gt; &lt;p/&gt; &quot;&#39;Black Pearl,&#39;&quot; her mother whispered through a respirator. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;What&#39;s &#39;Black Pearl&#39;?&quot; Cash asked.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;Send the manuscript to New York,&quot; her mother requested.&lt;p/&gt; That was 1992. Doctor&#39;s were telling Cash&#39;s mother, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Mary Ellen Cooper&quot;&gt;Mary Ellen Cooper&lt;/a&gt;, now 77, who had been in an auto accident, that she wouldn&#39;t walk again, but instead, the &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Stillwater (Oklahoma)&quot;&gt;Stillwater&lt;/a&gt;-based writer had her books on her mind.&lt;p/&gt; Today, both Marys laugh about this story. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;Black Pearl&quot; is a romance novel set in &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;India&quot;&gt;India&lt;/a&gt; about a young woman who was orphaned and walked across much of India in 1859. An editor expressed interest in publishing the book a couple of days before Cooper&#39;s accident. Cash delivered &quot;Black Pearl&quot; immediately, but it never was published. &lt;p/&gt; But that wouldn&#39;t set Cooper back.&lt;p/&gt; She would have 14 of her books either published or self-published after &quot;Black Pearl&quot; and would soon start work on a true-crime book, &quot;Blood and Pity.&quot; The back flap of the book reads, &quot;In the tradition of &#39;Sleeping With the Enemy,&#39; here&#39;s the terrifying true story of a conman-turned-killer who murdered his two wives â and possibly others.&quot; &lt;p/&gt; But Cooper&#39;s car accident would bring news almost as chilling as anything on the pages of &quot;Blood and Pity.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; Cooper said doctors told her she broke 19 bones.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;One doctor said, &#39;We&#39;re not working with broken bones, we&#39;re working with shattered bones,&#39;&quot; Cooper said. &quot;It&#39;s kind of odd. I never doubted I would recover.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; Cooper seems as if she&#39;s used to defying expectations. Cooper is the kind of person who&#39;s quick to pour a glass of cranberry juice, which matches the color of her sweater and pants, and won&#39;t hesitate talking about her grandchildren and extended family. &lt;p/&gt; Many of Cooper&#39;s books present a harsh contrast to the warm, endearing home she lives in and resembles.&lt;p/&gt; The same woman who wrote &quot;Fatal Trust&quot; and &quot;Deadly Patterns&quot; has numerous pictures of smiling family members hanging on her walls. &lt;p/&gt; She owns a rosary so large, it could fit around the necks of all 12 apostles. &lt;p/&gt; The board game &quot;Is the Pope Catholic? And Other Catholic Trivia&quot; sits atop one of the several bookshelves overflowing with literature. &lt;p/&gt; Nothing about the place points to a person interested in mystery or intrigue. &lt;p/&gt; But people turn to Cooper to tell their sometimes horrifying personal stories. She has interviewed hundreds of people, from ex-convicts to the mothers of murderers, to complete her stories. &lt;p/&gt; Cooper&#39;s car accident and the unpublished book &quot;Black Pearl&quot; are footnotes to the pages of her life.&lt;p/&gt; Before Cooper retired at 59 to become a full-time writer, she worked with her husband, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Charlie Cooper&quot;&gt;Charlie Cooper&lt;/a&gt;, to maintain a motorcycle shop, bicycle shop and locksmith business in Stillwater. The two shared a passion for motorcycles.&lt;p/&gt; She recalled her days working at a beauty shop in Stillwater before marrying Charlie in 1952. He would jump on his motorcycle and leave his family bike shop. When he passed the beauty shop, he would lean around the corner of W Sixth Avenue and S Main Street while his foot pegs sparked against the asphalt.&lt;p/&gt; This is the part of the story where Cooper puts her hands over her heart.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;I thought he was the most dashing, handsome man in &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Payne County&quot;&gt;Payne County&lt;/a&gt;,&quot; Cooper said.&lt;p/&gt; After getting married, Cooper managed the local motorcycle shop while her husband ran the bicycle and lock shop. Her eight children also kept her busy.&lt;p/&gt; Between staying on top of business matters and rearing the couple&#39;s eight children, Cooper didn&#39;t get much time to work on writing, but she read heavily.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;She has always been a multitasker,&quot; said &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Linda Bartram&quot;&gt;Linda Bartram&lt;/a&gt;, Cooper&#39;s daughter and owner of Cooper&#39;s Locksmith. &quot;When we were growing up, I remember her having a baby on her hip, a book in the hand (while) stirring a pot. That&#39;s just Mom, always reading.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; Cooper said starting her full-time writing career was rough.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;I&#39;d say (to my husband), &#39;You want to hear what I&#39;ve written?&#39;&quot; she asked. &lt;p/&gt; He replied with a no.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;He was not at all encouraging,&quot; Cooper laughed. &lt;p/&gt; Bartram remembered an article her mother wrote in the &#39;80s that combined several family road trips into one tale. The Coopers traveled in a large motor home nicknamed the Titanic. Bartram said during one trip the Titanic smashed into a black cow, and the animal embedded the motorcycle mounted to the front of the Titanic into the motor home&#39;s grill. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;From there, the trip went downhill,&quot; Bartram said.&lt;p/&gt; Running on a tight schedule, the family couldn&#39;t stop for repairs. The Coopers continued with the motorcycle stuck to the hood. It acted like a scary, expensive hood ornament all the way to &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Los Angeles&quot;&gt;Los Angeles&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;My dad didn&#39;t appreciate (her writing) that one,&quot; Bartram said.&lt;p/&gt; Cooper said her husband&#39;s attitude changed after her book &quot;Unlikely Assassins&quot; came out.&lt;p/&gt; In an &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Ohio&quot;&gt;Ohio&lt;/a&gt; hotel lobby, a woman hollered at Cooper and asked for an autograph. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;After that happened, he would start telling people, &#39;My wife writes books,&#39;&quot; Cooper said. &quot;Before that, he thought I was being silly.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; &quot;Unlikely Assassins&quot; wasn&#39;t a silly story. Cooper detailed the story of &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Francine Stepp&quot;&gt;Francine Stepp&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Cindy Lynn&quot;&gt;Cindy Lynn&lt;/a&gt;, two teens who murdered a Stillwater couple. On June 8, 1988, Mark and &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Delores Stepp&quot;&gt;Delores Stepp&lt;/a&gt; were found naked in their bedroom. &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Mark Stepp&quot;&gt;Mark Stepp&lt;/a&gt; had been shot, and the couple had been stabbed a combined 27 times.&lt;p/&gt; Cooper said she tried to get her son-in-law &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Billy Bartram&quot;&gt;Billy Bartram&lt;/a&gt;, one of the investigating officers at the time, to write a book about the case. She said he was sick of the case and never wanted to hear about it again.&lt;p/&gt; Cooper did. &lt;p/&gt; She said she began her work on the story the following fall. She interviewed teachers, sat through the court hearings and talked to several of the suspects&#39; friends. She even visited the &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Mabel Bassett Correctional Center&quot;&gt;Mabel Bassett Correctional Center&lt;/a&gt; in &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Oklahoma City&quot;&gt;Oklahoma City&lt;/a&gt; where the girls were held.&lt;p/&gt; Cooper also assists others in writing stories. Once a month, the Stillwater Writers&#39; Group meets to edit and discuss stories. Local science-fiction writer &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; title=&quot;Dennis Gronquist&quot;&gt;Dennis Gronquist&lt;/a&gt; has visited Cooper&#39;s home for writers&#39; group sessions for about eight years. &lt;p/&gt; &quot;It takes someone that cares and has patience (to help with writing),&quot; he said. &quot;She is such a moral support. She is the most important mentor I&#39;ve ever met.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; Not only has Cooper and her writing helped others, the books have helped Cooper, her daughter said.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;The books have been good for her,&quot; Bartram said. &quot;A lot of people shut themselves off from the world. She has kept her mind functioning by being a part of things.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; Although Cooper said she doesn&#39;t recall how many books she has sold, she does know why she writes.&lt;p/&gt; &quot;Many of the writers I know make a little bit (of money),&quot; Cooper said. &quot;I think (the important thing is) the satisfaction of seeing your work in print, knowing you researched it and wrote it. If somebody likes it, then it warms your heart.&quot;&lt;p/&gt; &lt;/span&gt; &lt;hr/&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;br/&gt; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; name=&quot;comments&quot;&gt; &lt;h3 class=&quot;bar color&quot;&gt;Leave a Comment&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;noscript&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;
