&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;table id=&quot;itemcontentlist&quot;&gt; &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.newschief.com/article/20100310/APS/1003101670&quot;&gt;AUTO RACING PACKAGE: Auto Racing Glance - The Ledger&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 10 Mar 2010 07:18 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;article_text article_paragraph1&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Schedule: Saturday, practice, qualifying (Versus, 2-3 p.m.); Sunday, race (Versus, 11:30 a.m.-2:30 p.m.).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Track: Streets of Sao Paulo (street course, 2.6 miles).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Race distance: 195 miles, 75 laps.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last year: Inaugural event.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Fast facts: Danica Patrick is back in her No. 7 Andretti Autosport ride after racing in three NASCAR Nationwide races and an ARCA event. ... Brazilian drivers Helio Castroneves, Tony Kanaan, Vitor Meira, Mario Romancini, Raphael Matos, Bia Figueiredo and Ana Beatriz are set to compete in the season-opening race, the country&#39;s first Indy-style event since the CART ran in Rio de Janeiro from 1996-2000. ... The circuit features a nearly mile-long straightaway and runs through the Anhembi Sambadrome, a stadium-like venue that is the site of Carnival parades. ... Dario Franchitti is the defending series champion. He won five times last year. ... Sao Paulo also will host the Formula One finale in November.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next race: Honda Grand Prix of St. Petersburg, March 28, Streets of St. Petersburg, Fla.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.indycar.com&quot;&gt;http://www.indycar.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;FORMULA ONE&amp;#13; Bahrain Grand Prix&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Site: Sakhir, Bahrain.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Schedule: Friday, practice (Speed, 6-7:30 a.m.); Saturday, practice and qualifying (Speed, 6-7:30 a.m.); Sunday, race (Speed, 7:30-10 a.m., 1:30-4 p.m.).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Track: Bahrain International (road course, 3.914 miles).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Race distance: 191.634 miles, 49 laps.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last year: Jenson Button raced to his third victory in the first four events of the season, beating Sebastian Vettel by 7.1 seconds. Button went on to win six of the first seven races and took the season title for Brawn GP.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Fast facts: Seven-time world champion Michael Schumacher is returning to racing after a three-year retirement. The 41-year-old German star, the winner of a record 91 races, is driving for Ross Brawn-led Mercedes GP. Schumacher won the first F1 race at the track in 2004. ... Lotus is returning to F1 after a 16-year absence, backed by the Malaysian government and a consortium of businessmen. Lotus won 79 races and seven constructors&#39; titles between 1958 and 1994. Jarno Trulli and Heikki Kovalainen will race for the team. ... Button is driving for McLaren.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next race: Australian Grand Grix, March 28, Albert Park, Melbourne, Australia.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.formula1.com&quot;&gt;http://www.formula1.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;NHRA FULL THROTTLE&amp;#13; NHRA Gatornationals&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Site: Gainesville, Fla.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Schedule: Friday, qualifying; Saturday, qualifying (ESPN2, Sunday, midnight-3 a.m.; Sunday, final eliminations (ESPN2, 6-9 p.m.).&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Track: Gainesville Raceway.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last year: Bob Tasca raced to his first career Funny Car victory. Larry Dixon (Top Fuel), Jason Line (Pro Stock) and Hector Arana (Pro Stock Motorcycle) also won.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last event: Cory McClenathan (Top Fuel) and Jack Beckman (Funny Car) won the rain-delayed NHRA Arizona Nationals on Feb. 22, an event marred by the death of a fan struck by a tire off Antron Brown&#39;s crashing Top Fuel car.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Fast facts: Kurt Busch, coming off a NASCAR Sprint Cup victory Sunday at Atlanta, is making his NHRA debut in the Super Gas class. He&#39;s driving his rebuilt &#39;70 Dodge Challenger, powered by a stroked 6.1-liter Hemi that produces 1,167 horsepower. ... Tire Kingdom is the title sponsor.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next event: NHRA Four-Wide Nationals, March 25-28, zMAX Dragway, Concord, N.C.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.nhra.com&quot;&gt;http://www.nhra.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;NASCAR&amp;#13; SPRINT CUP&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Last week: Kurt Busch won at Atlanta Motor Speedway, surviving two overtime restarts and 16 extra laps in the race marred by Carl Edwards&#39; retaliatory late-race bump that flipped Brad Keselowski&#39;s car.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next race: Food City 500, March 21, Bristol Motor Speedway, Bristol, Tenn.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.nascar.com&quot;&gt;http://www.nascar.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;NATIONWIDE&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Next race: Scotts Turf Builder 300, March 20, Bristol Motor Speedway, Bristol, Tenn.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last race: Kevin Harvick won at Las Vegas on Feb. 27, overcoming a pair of horrendous pit stops for his 35th Nationwide victory.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.nascar.com&quot;&gt;http://www.nascar.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;CAMPING WORLD TRUCKS&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Last week: Kevin Harvick won at Atlanta Motor Speedway. The Sprint Cup driver has won three straight starts in the series and five of his last nine.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Next race: Kroger 250, March 27, Martinsville Speedway, Martinsville, Va.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.nascar.com&quot;&gt;http://www.nascar.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;---&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3&gt;OTHER RACES&lt;/h3&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;WORLD OF OUTLAWS: Sprint Car, Texas Two Step, Friday, Lonestar Speedway, Kilgore, Texas, and Saturday, Houston Raceway Park, Baytown, Texas. On the Net: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.worldofoutlaws.com&quot;&gt;http://www.worldofoutlaws.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.insurancenewsnet.com/article.aspx?id=170263&amp;type=lifehealth&quot;&gt;Home Equity Impacts Retirement Planning More Than Stock Market Crash - Insurance News Net&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 10 Mar 2010 12:52 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;ctl00_BodyContent_art&quot; class=&quot;article_test&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;p class=&quot; bwtextaligncenter&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Americans&#39; Reluctance to Use Home Equity to Help Fund Retirement&lt;/i&gt;&lt;i&gt;Increases&amp;#13; Number &#39;At Risk&#39; by 10 Percentage Points&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; COLUMBUS, Ohio--(BUSINESS WIRE)--&amp;#13; More than 60 percent of households are &#39;at risk&#39; of being financially&amp;#13; unprepared for retirement, according to new research from the Center for&amp;#13; Retirement Research (CRR) at Boston College. The latest analysis of the&amp;#13; National Retirement Risk Index (NRRI), released today by the CRR and&amp;#13; underwritten by Nationwide Mutual Insurance Company, examines how not&amp;#13; taking full advantage of housing equity affects the share of U.S.&amp;#13; households &#39;at risk.&#39; The result is a 10 percentage-point rise in the&amp;#13; Index compared to just a seven-point increase from the 2008 stock market&amp;#13; crash.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The NRRI is a percentage measurement of how many working Americans are&amp;#13; &#39;at risk&#39; of being unable to maintain their standard of living in&amp;#13; retirement. The NRRI uses very conservative assumptions in its baseline&amp;#13; scenario. One of those assumptions is that consumers access their home&amp;#13; equity through a reverse mortgage and invest the proceeds in an&amp;#13; inflation-indexed annuity to help generate retirement income. The new&amp;#13; research removes that assumption.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &quot;Even after the bursting of the housing bubble, our research shows that&amp;#13; home equity remains a major financial asset and can significantly impact&amp;#13; retirement security,&quot; said Center Director Alicia H. Munnell. &quot;The&amp;#13; impact of home equity on the percent of households &#39;at risk&#39; is greater&amp;#13; than that of the recent stock market crash. How baby boomers and future&amp;#13; generations decide to use their home equity could determine how well&amp;#13; many fare in retirement.&quot;&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The full report is available at the Center&amp;#13; for Retirement Research at Boston College.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Creating Retirement Income&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &quot;Given the loss of pension plans and the uncertainty of Social Security,&amp;#13; retirees are undoubtedly going to shoulder more responsibility for&amp;#13; funding their retirement,&quot; said Brad Davis, vice president of retirement&amp;#13; income solutions for Nationwide Financial Services. &quot;If the last 18&amp;#13; months have taught us anything, it&#39;s that consumers need to resist&amp;#13; becoming overly dependent on any one asset, especially when taking into&amp;#13; account the unpredictable nature of the stock and real estate markets.&quot;&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Davis added, &quot;To face today&#39;s retirement challenges, consumers must be&amp;#13; open to utilizing all of their assets and consider working with a&amp;#13; financial professional who is prepared to handle the task of developing&amp;#13; a comprehensive retirement income strategy.&quot;&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Davis noted that financial&amp;#13; professionals understand they need to be prepared to help clients&amp;#13; transition from asset accumulation to income generation in retirement.&amp;#13; According to research from the Financial Planning Association, more than&amp;#13; 89 percent of financial professionals say they are likely to obtain more&amp;#13; training on ways to generate retirement&amp;#13; income.&lt;sup&gt;1&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &quot;We encourage financial professionals to seek out the education and&amp;#13; support they need to deal with this very critical phase of an investor&#39;s&amp;#13; life by partnering with financial institutions that have the strategies&amp;#13; and resources to help them manage the challenges retirees will face in&amp;#13; the upcoming decades,&quot; said Davis.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; To help financial professionals with income planning, Nationwide created RetireSense&lt;sup&gt;Â®&lt;/sup&gt;.&amp;#13; RetireSense is an innovative investment and draw-down strategy that&amp;#13; helps investment professionals address their clients&#39; individual needs.&amp;#13; It provides them with a clear road map for retirement income planning&amp;#13; that helps identify which investments to consider harvesting for income,&amp;#13; and when to do so.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;About the National Retirement Risk Index&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The NRRI was developed by the Center for Retirement Research at Boston&amp;#13; College and underwritten by a grant from Nationwide.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The Index projects how much income households are expected to have in&amp;#13; retirement relative to their pre-retirement income. It then compares&amp;#13; this &#39;replacement rate&#39; to a target rate that would allow a household to&amp;#13; maintain its pre-retirement standard of living. Households that fall&amp;#13; more than 10 percent short of the target are considered &#39;at risk.&#39;&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The Index produces conservative estimates by assuming that people work&amp;#13; to age 65, annuitize all of their financial assets, and receive income&amp;#13; from reverse mortgages on their homes. More realistic assumptions&amp;#13; regarding earlier retirement and the reluctance of people to annuitize&amp;#13; their assets or tap housing equity â as illustrated in the new research&amp;#13; â would put the percentage of workers &#39;at risk&#39; higher.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Nationwide&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Nationwide, based in Columbus, Ohio, is one of the largest and strongest&amp;#13; diversified insurance and financial services organizations in the U.S.&amp;#13; and is rated A+ by A.M. Best. The company provides a full range of&amp;#13; personalized insurance and financial services, including auto insurance,&amp;#13; motorcycle, boat, homeowners, life&amp;#13; insurance, farm, commercial insurance, administrative services,&amp;#13; annuities, mortgages, mutual funds, pensions, long-term savings plans&amp;#13; and health and productivity services. For more information, visit nationwide.com.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;Brad Davis is a registered representative of Nationwide Investment&amp;#13; Services Corporation, member FINRA. &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://venturebeat.com/2010/03/09/true-crime/&quot;&gt;Activision Blizzard shows off footage from True Crime reboot - Venturebeat.com&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 10 Mar 2010 01:13 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;entry single-entry&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://venturebeat.com/2010/03/09/true-crime/truecrime_vb_4/&quot;&gt;&lt;img class=&quot;alignleft size-medium wp-image-166594&quot; src=&quot;http://venturebeat.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/03/TrueCrime_VB_4-300x168.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; width=&quot;300&quot; height=&quot;168&quot;/&gt; &lt;/a&gt;Re-entering the highly competitive &quot;sandbox&quot; crime genre made famous by Rockstar&#39;s Grand Theft Auto series, Activision Blizzard&#39;s Activision Publishing division today showed live gameplay footage of its reboot entrÃ©e, True Crime, at the Game Developers Conference in San Francisco.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Many thought the series dead after a disappointing critical and fiscal second effort in 2006 with the second in the series, True Crime: New York. But Activision tapped United Front Games (maker of &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://games.venturebeat.com/2010/03/04/modnation-racers-blends-infinite-modding-and-goofy-kart-racing-video/&quot;&gt;ModNation Racers&lt;/a&gt;). With former employees from Radical Games, EA&#39;s Need for Speed franchise, and Rockstar Games, UFG has been in development with its own unique software tools to generate the third-person perspective, Hong Kong-based game.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Activision is trying to differentiate its title from the towering success of Grand Theft Auto IV and, to a lesser extent, THQ&#39;s well-received Saints Row, by focusing on deep combat moves and an undercover-cop story generated by extensive research done with the Hong Kong police department and active members from the Triad crime organization.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;We&#39;re treating the franchise as if it were a brand new [intellectual property],&quot; said Lead Producer Jeff O&#39;Connell. &quot;True Crime is being developed by a completely new team using new tech, and a brand new storyline that&#39;s serious, not campy.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;In the early (pre-alpha testing) version shown at the W Hotel, Activision demoed a fully working game offering with smooth transitions between exploration, open-world car chases, and hand-to-hand combat. Visually, the game reflects a relatively modern-looking Hong Kong, packed with dense skyscrapers, night-time marketplaces, and bustling streets. Gamers will play detective Wei Shen, an undercover cop who reports to a hot-headed, foul-mouthed crime boss &quot;Winston&quot; of the Triads whose mother and family have been threatened by a rival club. At this point in development, character facial movement and animations aren&#39;t fully complete, and they looked slightly out of sync. But the game is due in fall of this year, meaning UFG has several months to develop and hone it. Character movement, particularly in combat interaction, was more impressive.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The first and only mission shown is to confront a rival gang at their manufacturing plant and remove everyone except Siu Wah, a key member of the gang. You&#39;ll have to locate, capture, and usher him out of the building as enemies swarm in upon learning of your attack. One of the more impressive scenes takes place after you successfully leave the building. On a stolen cop motorcycle you&#39;ll chase Wah in a stolen cop car, leap from the bike onto the car&#39;s roof, climb into the car, and force Wah to surrender.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;We spent several weeks earning the trust of one real-life Triad members,&quot; said O&#39;Connell. &quot;Once we were able to gain their trust, they showed us a lot. They drove us around the city, showed us their street fighting techniques, and helped us piece together how their organization works.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Players will encounter a combat system that looks on the surface to resemble Midway&#39;s John Woo-influenced Strangehold game, with an impressive array of environmental combat opportunities. Taking the combat a little further than competitive titles, UFG has clearly studied Jackie Chan films too. Live electrical boxes, open garbage cans, refrigerator doors â used to slam enemies in the face â stair banisters and tables are used for sliding and creating combination attacks as an advantage to confront un-even odds. You&#39;ll wield a number of weapons from hand guns to Uzis, plus bloodier weapons, such as meat cleavers.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;Unlike the way the West perceives Hong Kong, the city isn&#39;t a wild, crime-filled place,&quot; O&#39;Connell said. &quot;There are very strict gun laws enforced there. You can get arrested for holding a single bullet. So we had to sex up the city. And that&#39;s why the meat cleaver and chopping knives play a heavy role in combat. &#39;Chopping&#39; is a real technique employed to show examples of those who cross the local Triads.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;True Crime provides a linear story with many options to take on &quot;jobs&quot; and missions that build up characters&#39; &quot;face.&quot; Face is equivalent to &quot;respect,&quot; a system in the game that enables players to use to open additional side missions. Side missions feature the ability to date girls (with the possibility of &quot;tasteful&quot; romantic scenes), upgrade your look with accessories such as new hair styles, clothes, watches, better cars, and the ability to get into otherwise closed night clubs.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;We haven&#39;t announced the voice talent we are working with, but you will be able to date girls who are played by popular actresses who we believe players will want to &#39;date&#39; in the game,&quot; said O&#39;Connell.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;With an intense hand-to-hand combat system, arcade-style driving, and an serious, non-campy storyline (&quot;there will no zombies, dragons, or flaming skulls&quot; O&#39;Connell said), Activision hopes to re-energize the True Crime brand in the tough-to-crack, GTA-dominated genre.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p id=&quot;story_next_prev&quot;&gt;Next Story: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://venturebeat.com/2010/03/09/google-apps-marketplace-expensify/&quot;&gt;What&#39;s next for Google&#39;s Apps Marketplace â contextual gadgets and more&lt;/a&gt; &lt;br /&gt;Previous Story: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://venturebeat.com/2010/03/09/google-apps-marketplace/&quot;&gt;Google launches a store for business apps&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 10 Mar 2010 01:21 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;interior-depth&quot;&gt;&lt;p align=&quot;left&quot;&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;KonaBody&quot;&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;b&gt;Bangalore, Mar 10 : TVS Motor Company targets to sell two million two-wheelers in 2010-11, Company Vice-President (Sales and Marketing) R Dilip said today.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Talking to newspersons here, he said in the current fourth quarter the company was expected to achieve a 30 per cent growth on Year-on-Year basis. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Announcing the launch of TVS Jive, he said with the launch of the country&#39;s first auto-clutch motorcycle the market share of the company in the two-wheeler segment was expected to increase by 10 per cent from the present 20 per cent. About 20,000 units were sold per month.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;He said the new TVS Jive, targetted at salaried and business class, is propelled by a 110 cc engine which features innovative T-matic technology, patent of which was awaited, with rotary gear technology coupled with an automatic clutch.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;He said the unique feature of TVS Jive being its anti-stall mechanism which makes smooth riding possible at low speeds even in high gears, without the engine shutting off.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;TVS Jive priced at Rs 41,735 ex-showroom in Bangalore was available in blue, black and red colours. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#3&quot;&gt;Honda to build second motorcycle plant in India - YAHOO!&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#4&quot;&gt;Honda India bike unit plans $103 mil second plant - Reuters India&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;table id=&quot;itemcontentlist&quot;&gt; &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://bworldonline.com/main/content.php?id=7420&quot;&gt;BPI Family Bank sees robust auto loan growth in 2010 - BusinessWorld Online&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 09 Mar 2010 07:48 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;linkbox&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br class=&quot;clearboth&quot;/&gt;   &lt;/p&gt;&lt;h6&gt;Story tools&lt;/h6&gt; &lt;/div&gt;  &lt;h5&gt;Finance&lt;/h5&gt;&lt;p class=&quot;byline&quot;&gt;Posted on 08:44 PM, March 09, 2010&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p class=&quot;byline&quot;/&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;BPI FAMILY Savings Bank, the thrift lending arm of listed Bank of the Philippine Islands (BPI), expects its auto loans to grow by double digits this year as consumer confidence recovers along with the economy.&lt;/b&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Felipe P. Carlos, BPI Family vice-president and head of retail auto loans, told a briefing yesterday: &quot;Last year, everybody was hesitant [to spend] and held off purchases because they were worried about the recession... [But that&#39;s not the case now]. Even industry figures will show that.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The Chamber of Automotive Manufacturers of the Philippines, Inc. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; reported yesterday that car sales in the first two months of the year surged by 36.6% to 24,366 units.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; David G. Sarmiento, Jr., BPI Family senior vice-president for auto and motorcycle loans, said the bank&#39;s auto loans grew by about 27% in the first two months of the year -- enough to purchase about 3,000 vehicles -- but he declined to disclose the actual loan amount.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Despite the higher auto loan growth numbers in the early part of the year, BPI Family executives said they expect the bank&#39;s 2010 auto loan portfolio, which reached almost P20 billion last year, to increase by 10%-12% since it was still too early to establish a trend.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Mr. Sarmiento said the introduction of new car models is expected to spur loan growth, with vehicle owners seeking to replace old car models.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Also yesterday, BPI Family launched a promo extending free comprehensive insurance that also covers &quot;acts of God&quot; incidents to cars purchased using a BPI loan. The cars must be purchased by March 31 and for delivery up to April 15.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Mr. Sarmiento said the bank expects a good reception to the promo, pointing out that auto loan applications surged when the program was first introduced in August 2008.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Meanwhile, BPI/MS Insurance Corp., a joint venture between BPI and Japan&#39;s largest non-life insurance firm Mitsui Sumitomo Insurance Co., said it had paid about P500 million in claims from damage caused by typhoons Ondoy and Pepeng.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Perfecto M. Domingo, head of underwriting and claims group at BPI/MS, added the company expects its 2010 revenues from premium payments to grow by 10% from P2.7 billion last year. &quot;[The main growth driver] are motor and fire insurance and also bancassurance business coming from BPI,&quot; he said. -- &lt;b&gt;Don Gil K. Carreon&lt;/b&gt;   &lt;/p&gt; &lt;div align=&quot;center&quot;&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; href=&quot;#top&quot;&gt;Back to top&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. href=&quot;http://www.earthtimes.org/articles/show/aarp-selects-restaurantcom-as-a,1197213.shtml&quot;&gt;AARP Selects Restaurant.com as a Preferred Provider to Make Delicious ... - Earthtimes&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 09 Mar 2010 07:55 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;dfont&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;Relationship Gives AARP Members a New Discount on Gift Certificates for More than 14,000 Restaurants Nationwide&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;WASHINGTON&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-chron&quot;&gt;March 9&lt;/span&gt; /PRNewswire-USNewswire/ --&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;AARP and Restaurant.com today announced a new relationship that will make an exclusive discount available to AARP members on the 25,000 daily gift certificate options offered on Restaurant.com. The new AARP Restaurant Discount Center powered by Restaurant.com is available by visiting (&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.aarp.org/restaurant&quot;&gt;www.aarp.org/restaurant&lt;/a&gt;). The site allows AARP members to search a database of more than 14,000 participating restaurants at which they can receive savings and enjoy memorable meals.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;(Logo: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.newscom.com/cgi-bin/prnh/20070209/NYF043LOGO&quot;&gt;http://www.newscom.com/cgi-bin/prnh/20070209/NYF043LOGO&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;Our members lead active and engaging lives: they&#39;re traveling, visiting their kids and grandkids and spending time with friends,&quot; said &lt;span class=&quot;xn-person&quot;&gt;Howard Byck&lt;/span&gt;, senior vice president of lifestyle products and services for AARP Services, Inc., the wholly-owned subsidiary of AARP. &quot;Particularly in this economy, AARP is committed to helping them enjoy more for less. Launching the Restaurant Discount Center powered by Restaurant.com is a natural fit that gives AARP members access to discounts at thousands of restaurants across the country.&quot; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Since 1999, Restaurant.com has connected restaurants and diners nationwide. ThroughÂ this new relationship,Â AARP membersÂ can access discounts forÂ Restaurant.comÂ gift certificatesÂ by visiting the Restaurant Discount Center and,Â when prompted,Â entering their AARP member information. SavingsÂ apply to the Restaurant.com Gift Center and to all theÂ gift certificate denominations available on the site, which include &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$10&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$25&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$50&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$75&lt;/span&gt; and &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$100&lt;/span&gt;.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &quot;Restaurant.com is proud to be an AARP preferred discount provider. AARP is a reputable organization that provides so much value to an important population,&quot; said &lt;span class=&quot;xn-person&quot;&gt;Cary Chessick&lt;/span&gt;, president and CEO of Restaurant.com. &quot;Like AARP, Restaurant.com believes in quality products and services and we look forward to making a best-in-class experience available to AARP members as they take advantage of dining savings through this new relationship.&quot; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;To explore all the restaurant choices in any local or national area, AARP members can simply select a location and then choose to refine their restaurant search by criteria such as cuisine, price and atmosphere. Once a specific restaurant is selected, restaurant Web pages show menus, photos, gift certificate denominations and available quantities. Members can then purchase the denomination and quantity of their choice, print the certificate instantly for immediate use and present the certificate to their server to have the amount deducted from the final bill.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;For more information on the Restaurant Discount Center, AARP members can visit &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.restaurantdiscountcenter.com/&quot;&gt;www.aarp.org/restaurant&lt;/a&gt; or call 1-877-657-4710. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;About AARP &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;AARP is a nonprofit, nonpartisan membership organization that helps people 50+ have independence, choice and control in ways that are beneficial and affordable to them and society as a whole. AARP does not endorse candidates for public office or make contributions to either political campaigns or candidates. We produce AARP The Magazine, the definitive voice for 50+ Americans and the world&#39;s largest-circulation magazine with over 35.7 million readers; AARP Bulletin, the go-to news source for AARP&#39;s millions of members and Americans 50+; AARP Segunda Juventud, the only bilingual U.S. publication dedicated exclusively to the 50+ Hispanic community; and our website, AARP.org. AARP Foundation is an affiliated charity that provides security, protection, and empowerment to older persons in need with support from thousands of volunteers, donors, and sponsors. We have staffed offices in all 50 states, the &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;District of Columbia&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;Puerto Rico&lt;/span&gt;, and the &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;U.S. Virgin Islands&lt;/span&gt;.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;ABOUT AARP SERVICES INC.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;AARP Services Inc., founded in 1999, is a wholly-owned taxable subsidiary of AARP. AARP Services manages the provider relationships for and performs quality control oversight of the wide range of products and services that carry the AARP name and are made available by independent providers as benefits to AARP&#39;s almost 40 million members. The provider offers currently span health products, travel and leisure products, and life event services. Specific products include Medicare supplemental insurance; member discounts on rental cars, cruises, vacation packages and lodging; special offers on technology and gifts; pharmacy services; legal services; and long-term care insurance. AARP Services also engages in new product development activities for AARP and provides certain consulting services to outside companies. In 2005, AARP Services founded AARP Financial Inc., a wholly-owned taxable subsidiary that manages the provider relationships for and performs quality control oversight for the financial products that carry the AARP name, including credit cards, auto and home, mobile home and motorcycle insurance, and life insurance and annuities. AARP Financial also provides access to proprietary investment products and services, including mutual funds and financial guidance, designed to meet the needs of investors at any life stage.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;About Restaurant.com&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;Restaurant.com is the trusted and valued source connecting restaurants and diners nationwide. The company offers savings at more than 14,000 restaurants nationwide with more than 25,000 daily gift certificate options. Restaurant.com brings people together to relax, converse and enjoy well-prepared and -served meals at affordable prices. To date, Restaurant.com customers have saved more than &lt;span class=&quot;xn-money&quot;&gt;$100 million&lt;/span&gt; through the gift certificate program. Restaurant.com has operated since 1999 and is based in &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;Arlington Heights, Ill.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;SOURCE AARP&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. class=&quot;entry-title bookmark&quot;&gt;Ohio St.: Employee kills co-worker, wounds another (AP)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;updated&quot;&gt;40 seconds ago &lt;span class=&quot;value&quot;&gt;2010-03-09T08:44:24-08:00&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;4&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://in.reuters.com/article/businessNews/idINIndia-46761020100309&quot;&gt;Honda India bike unit plans $103 mil second plant - Reuters India&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 09 Mar 2010 12:46 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;resizeableText&quot;&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_start&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;articleLocation&quot;&gt;MUMBAI &lt;/span&gt;(Reuters) - Japan&#39;s Honda will invest 4.7 billion rupees ($103 million) to build a second production plant in India, with an annual capacity of 600,000 units, to meet rising demand in the world&#39;s second-largest motorcycle market.&lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_byline&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_0&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Motorcycle sales in India rose 19 percent in 2009 to nearly 9 million units, behind China&#39;s 15 million-plus units.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_1&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Honda Motorcycle &amp;amp; Scooter India Pvt Ltd said in a statement the new plant, to be located in the north-western Rajasthan state, would become operational from the second half of 2011.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_2&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Honda&#39;s Indian unit said it would also expand capacity at its existing plant in Haryana state to 1.55 million units by end-March from 1.25 million units and further raise it to 1.6 million units next year.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_3&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; The company, which produces Unicorn, Shine, CBF Stunner motorcycles and scooters including Activa and Aviator, said its annual production capacity would rise to 2.2 million units, once the second plant becomes operational.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_4&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Honda, which had so far been producing bikes with engine capacity of more than 125cc, last month made its entry into the 100-110cc segment with the launch of CB Twister.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_5&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Honda Motorcycle is not the only one expanding in India.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_6&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Hero Honda Motors, the country&#39;s largest bike maker in which Honda has a 26-percent stake, has also said that it was looking at setting up a new plant and expanding capacity from its current 5 million units a year.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_7&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;p&gt; Earlier this month, smaller rival Bajaj Auto said it was expanding its motorcycle capacity to 300,000 units per month by April 2010, up from its current just over 200,000 units month. &lt;span class=&quot;label&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;Continued...&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;midArticle_8&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://biz.yahoo.com/bw/100308/20100308005795.html?.v=1&quot;&gt;Research and Markets: the US Motorcycle Manufacturing Industry ... - Yahoo Finance&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 08 Mar 2010 06:31 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;y-article-bd&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;DUBLIN--(BUSINESS WIRE)--&lt;b&gt;Research and Markets&lt;/b&gt;(&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://cts.businesswire.com/ct/CT?id=smartlink&amp;amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F6fe934%2Fmotorcycle_manufac&amp;amp;esheet=6205620&amp;amp;lan=en_US&amp;amp;anchor=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F6fe934%2Fmotorcycle_manufac&amp;amp;index=1&amp;amp;md5=f7b1a15ee464fd2e7a6ae09a433e880c&quot;&gt;http://www.researchandmarkets.com/research/6fe934/motorcycle_manufac&lt;/a&gt;) has announced the addition of the &quot;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://cts.businesswire.com/ct/CT?id=smartlink&amp;amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F6fe934%2Fmotorcycle_manufac&amp;amp;esheet=6205620&amp;amp;lan=en_US&amp;amp;anchor=Motorcycle+Manufacturing&amp;amp;index=2&amp;amp;md5=3b4ed675c8031c14053997b46bc413f2&quot;&gt;Motorcycle Manufacturing&lt;/a&gt;&quot; report to their offering.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;First Research is the leading industry intelligence company that helps sales teams perform faster and smarter, open doors, and close more deals. First Research performs the &quot;heavy lifting&quot; by synthesizing hundreds of sources into an easy to digest format that a sales person can consume very quickly to better understand a prospect&#39;s business issues.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Executive Summary&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Brief Excerpt from Industry Overview Chapter:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The US motorcycle manufacturing industry includes about 60 companies with combined annual revenue of about $6 billion. The industry, which is highly concentrated, is dominated by Harley-Davidson . Other industry participants include foreign-based companies with final assembly operations in the US, parts and accessories manufacturers, and custom builders who make built-to-order products for motorcycle enthusiasts.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;COMPETITIVE LANDSCAPE&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Personal income and interest rates drive demand. Motorcycles are considered discretionary items in the US since few are used as a primary means of transportation. About one fourth of motorcycle purchases are financed. The profitability of individual companies depends on volume and sales of high-margin accessories and add-ons. Small manufacturers compete by offering highly customized products. Annual sales per employee averages about $400,000.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;PRODUCTS, OPERATIONS &amp;amp; TECHNOLOGY&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Major products include touring and cruiser motorcycles designed for comfort and long distance rides (67 percent of industry revenue); off-road cycles designed for dirt and mountain terrain (25 percent); dual sport designed for both road and off-road usage (3 percent); and scooters (5 percent). Motorcycle engines are measured in cubic centimeters (cc) and range from 50cc to 2300cc. Heavyweight bikes have engines with 650cc or greater.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Motorcycles are typically produced on assembly lines, similar to how the auto industry makes cars. Parts are received from outside sources (either third-party companies or other corporate-owned plants), usually on a just-in-time basis.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Key Topics Covered:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p/&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt; Industry Overview &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Quarterly Industry Update &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Business Challenges &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Trends AND Opportunities &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Call Preparation Questions &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Financial Information &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Industry Forecast &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Website and Media Links &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; Glossary of Acronyms &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;For more information visit &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://cts.businesswire.com/ct/CT?id=smartlink&amp;amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F6fe934%2Fmotorcycle_manufac&amp;amp;esheet=6205620&amp;amp;lan=en_US&amp;amp;anchor=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchandmarkets.com%2Fresearch%2F6fe934%2Fmotorcycle_manufac&amp;amp;index=3&amp;amp;md5=e3a369a10e8f42ce164c2410fd272331&quot;&gt;http://www.researchandmarkets.com/research/6fe934/motorcycle_manufac&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Source: First Research&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;http://cts.businesswire.com/ct/CT?id=bwnews&amp;amp;sty=20100308005795r1&amp;amp;sid=yatoo&amp;amp;distro=nx&quot;/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;bwct31415&quot;&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.gazettetimes.com/online/events-calendar/article_2977758c-28f4-11df-bee9-001cc4c002e0.html&quot;&gt;Datebook business calendar (March 8) - Corvallis Gazette-Times&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 08 Mar 2010 07:49 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;blox-story-text&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Business calendar published Monday, March 8, 2010:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Today:&lt;/strong&gt; A &lt;strong&gt;property-casualty pre-licensing class&lt;/strong&gt; for insurance professionals will be offered through the Linn-Benton Community College Small Business Development Center and PacWest Insurance School. Classes will be 8 a.m. to 5 p.m. today through Friday on the second floor of the Calapooia Center, LBCC, 6500 Pacific Blvd. S.W., Albany. This 40-hour class is a State of Oregon required class that allows the licensee to take the state examination to sell auto, home, boat, motorcycle, RV and commercial lines of insurance. For more information or to register, contact the PacWest Insurance School at 541-971-9566.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Tuesday&lt;/strong&gt;: &lt;strong&gt;Corvallis Chamber of Commerce Greeters&lt;/strong&gt;, 8:30 to 9:30 a.m., hosted by Downtown Dental, 142 S.W. Second St.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Tuesday&lt;/strong&gt;: &lt;strong&gt;Employer&#39;s Guide to Civil Rights Laws and Workplace Harassment&lt;/strong&gt;, educational seminar, 8:30 a.m. to noon, Central Willamette Community Credit Union headquarters, Albany. Presenter: Jennifer Germundson, the Bureau of Labor and Industries manager of technical assistance for employers. To avoid claims of workplace harassment and discrimination, managers and supervisors need to understand the protections under state and federal civil rights law. Learn about protected classes, recognizing unlawful behavior, conducting an investigation, communicating policies and expectations to employers, and BOLI enforcement policies. Cost: $59 per person, or $49 per Albany, Corvallis or Lebanon Chamber of Commerce members. To register, contact Greg Ivers, 541-967-2171, Ext. 264, or greg.e.ivers@state.or.us.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Tuesday: Ribbon cutting&lt;/strong&gt;, 9:45 to 10:15 a.m., Springhill Country Club, 155 Country Club Lane, Albany.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Thursday: Downtown After Hours&lt;/strong&gt;, 5:30 to 7 p.m., Mod Pod, 115 N.W. Second St. The Downtown Corvallis Association&#39;s monthly networking social provides an opportunity to get acquainted with DCA members in a relaxed atmosphere. Those attending are asked to bring an item for a prize drawing.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Friday: &quot;Become a Legacy Family Business,&quot;&lt;/strong&gt; 7:30 to 9:30 a.m., Allison Inn &amp;amp; Spa, 2525 Allison Lane, Newberg. Presented by the Austin Family Business Program, College of Business at Oregon State University. Author/expert Dr. Lee Hausner, senior managing director of First Foundation Advisors and internationally recognized business consultant and family wealth adviser, will give the keynote address. Cost: $35. Register at &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.familybusinessonline.org&quot;&gt;www.familybusinessonline.org&lt;/a&gt;. For more information, call 541-737-3326 or 800-859-7609.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Saturday&lt;/strong&gt;: A noncredit &lt;strong&gt;traffic control flagger certification course&lt;/strong&gt; will take place from 8 a.m. to 12:30 p.m. in the Fireside Room, Calapooia Center, Linn-Benton Community College, 6500 Pacific Blvd. S.W. in Albany. After meeting all requirements, students can be certified to flag traffic in Oregon, Idaho, Montana and Washington. Job-finding information will be provided in class. Cost: $80, includes all materials, certification test and card. Minimum qualifications: at least 18 years of age and possess a valid driver&#39;s license. For more information or to register, call the LBCC Business, Healthcare and Workforce Division at 541-917-4923.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;April 12 and 13: Oregon Employer Council Annual State Conference for Business&lt;/strong&gt;, the Nines Hotel, Portland. The conference is open to all business people, and will cover topics of importance to business owners, managers, supervisors and human resource professionals. Continuing education credits are offered. Early registration fee: $279, includes education sessions and handouts, most meals, and networking opportunities. After March 12, fee is $329. One-day fees available. For more information and to register, see &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.OEC.org&quot;&gt;www.OEC.org&lt;/a&gt;, or call Marney Roddick, 503-947-1305.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.hindustantimes.com/business-news/auto/India-s-car-sales-up-33-per-cent-in-February/Article1-516668.aspx&quot;&gt;India&#39;s car sales up 33 per cent in February - Hindustan Times&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 08 Mar 2010 06:31 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ni&quot; id=&quot;mainstory2&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Anticipation of a price hike after the budget pushed car sales in India in February this year.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;A total of 153,845 vehicles were sold as their sales went up by 33 percent in February, according to data released by the Society of Indian Automobile Manufacturers (SIAM) Monday. Car manufacturers sold 115,505 units in the year-ago period. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Sale of commercial vehicles, a key indicator of economic activity, rose a whopping 87 percent during the month at 58,024 units. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Motorcycle sales, which constitute bulk of the two-wheeler segment, also were up by 30.7 percent at 642,419 units compared to 491,451 units in the corresponding month last year. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Auto stocks reacted positively to the news and were among the major gainers on the Bombay Stock Exchange. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;During the April-February period, sales of passenger vehicles increased 26.13 percent and that of commercial vehicles rose 35.2 percent. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee had announced a two percent hike in excise tax on prices of large cars, and sports and multi-utility vehicles in the general budget presented on february 26. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;The government had offered excise duty relief to car makers as a stimulus in 2008 when auto sales dropped following a slowdown in the economy after recession hit the world. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;The excise duty was slashed on two-wheelers (from 10 percent to 8 percent), small cars (from 12 percent to 8 percent) and big cars (from 24 percent to 20 percent). &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Major car manufacturers have raised prices of cars by up to Rs.25,000 reacting to the increase in central excise duty, which is now at 10 percent. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Also, prospective buyers may be in for another round of price hike as the country is set to adopt new emission norms compliant auto fuel, Euro IV, by April 1 in 13 metro cities.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;4&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.businessweek.com/news/2010-03-08/hero-honda-may-add-fourth-plant-on-india-rural-sales-update2-.html&quot;&gt;Hero Honda May Add Fourth Plant on India Rural Sales (Update2) - BusinessWeek&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 08 Mar 2010 02:27 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;story-body&quot; class=&quot;clearfix&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;span id=&quot;pubDate&quot; class=&quot;date&quot;&gt;March 08, 2010, 5:33 AM EST&lt;/span&gt; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; (Adds shares rose to record in the sixth paragraph.)&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;By Subramaniam Sharma&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; March 8 (Bloomberg) -- Hero Honda Motors Ltd., maker of half the motorcycles sold in India, may build a fourth factory as it targets rural markets and possible exports to Africa.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; The company will decide on the new factory within six months, Managing Director Pawan Kant Munjal, 55, said in an interview in New Delhi. It hopes to reach an agreement this year with partner Honda Motor Co. on starting African sales, he said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; To help win sales among India&#39;s more than 740 million rural residents, Hero Honda has set up health-care initiatives and services to guide people in getting driving licenses. Coupled with motorcycle tax cuts and economic growth, the programs helped Hero Honda boost sales 24 percent in the past 11 months.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &quot;The market will continue to grow and it makes sense to invest money,&quot; said Juergen Maier, who helps manage 860 million euros ($1.1 billion) of assets, including Hero Honda shares, at Raiffeisen Capital Management in Vienna. Expanding in rural areas now &quot;is a huge advantage&quot; over overseas companies such as Yamaha Motor Co., he said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Bajaj Auto Ltd., India&#39;s second-biggest motorcycle maker, has also boosted its focus on rural areas as Prime Minister Manmohan Singh boost spending on new roads and infrastructure for villages as part of his &#39;Build India&#39; campaign.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Hero Honda rose 2.3 percent to a record close of 1,913.9 rupees in Mumbai today. The shares have gained 11 percent this year after more than doubling last year.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;center&quot;&gt; Rural Focus&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Hero Honda is considering a plant that can make 2,000 units daily and will fund the plan using its own cash, Munjal said during the March 4 interview. The company, 26 percent-owned by Tokyo-based Honda, can now make 5 million motorcycles and scooters a year. Hero Group, founded by Munjal&#39;s father and uncles, holds a 29 percent stake in the motorcycle-maker.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Hero Honda expects to sell 50 percent of its motorcycles in villages in the next three to five years, from about 40 percent now, Munjal said. The company three years ago started a marketing initiative called &#39;Har Gaon, Har Angan,&#39; or &#39;Every Village, Every Courtyard&#39;, to increase sales in villages with a population of more than 5,000 people.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &quot;The government has a clear cut long-term focus because a large portion of the population lives out there,&quot; said Munjal. &quot;A lot of activity is going on in rural areas. I expect a higher percentage of growth coming from rural areas.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; The company is also diversifying by aiming to boost exports, which now account for 2.2 percent of annual sales. By contrast, Bajaj Auto sells 33 percent of two-wheelers overseas. The bulk of Hero Honda&#39;s exports are to Sri Lanka, Bangladesh and Columbia. Bajaj sell motorcycles in countries including Nigeria, Angola, Uganda and Kenya.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;center&quot;&gt; &#39;Wider Canvas&#39;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Hero Honda is trying to convince Honda to allow it to enter more export markets, Munjal said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &quot;We are getting close to being able to work out a deal where we can start going into Africa,&quot; said Munjal. &quot;We want to establish ourselves in the international market so we have a wider canvas.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Simultaneously, Hero Honda is expanding its rural reach in India by adding about 500 more dealerships, service centers and other outlets across the country. The company currently has more than 4,000 facilities nationwide, including about 700 dealers.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; Close to 70 percent of India&#39;s population of more than 1.1 billion live in villages and they contribute about 45 percent of the economy, according to a 2008 study by National Council of Applied Economic Research.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; About 10 percent of the people living in villages in India own a motorcycle, compared with the national average of 18 percent, local brokerage Batlivala &amp;amp; Karani Securities Ltd. said in a report last month.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;--With assistance from Manish Modi in New Delhi. Editors: Anand Krishnamoorthy, Ian Rowley&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;To contact the reporter on the story: Subramaniam Sharma in New Delhi at ssharma@bloomberg.net;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;To contact the editor responsible for this story: Neil Denslow at ndenslow@bloomberg.net&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;h4&gt;Related Articles&lt;/h4&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;.
