Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.azdailysun.com/news/national/article_ceea4af2-1ccd-55e6-abb1-b620ca898533.html&quot;&gt;Trio shot to death in Chicago home - Arizona Daily Sun&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 03 Mar 2010 05:04 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;blox-story-text&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;DARIEN, Ill. (MCT) -- A husband, wife and their son were found shot to death in their Chicago- area home early Tuesday morning after the couple&#39;s daughter called police while hiding in a closet, officials said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Police arrived at the house in the western suburb of Darien, Ill, shortly after 1 a.m. MST and discovered the bodies of Jeffrey Kramer, 50, his wife Lori Kramer, 46, and their son Michael, 20, according to Darien Police Chief Robert Pavelchik.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Jeffrey and Michael were found on the first floor and Lori was on a stairway leading up to the second floor, Pavelchik said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Police found three other people in the home: the couple&#39;s daughter Angela, 25, who had called 911; the couple&#39;s oldest son, Anthony, 29, who was climbing out a basement window when officers arrived; and a 17-year-old girlfriend of Michael whom police would not identify. They said she was the one neighbors reported pounding on their doors after the shootings.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The eldest son apparently had his bedroom in the basement, Pavelchik said, explaining why he was crawling out of the window.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Officers were talking to all three at the police station, Pavelchik said, but none of the them is being regarded as a suspect.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;All three victims were shot but no weapon has been found in the house so far, he said. &quot;If it&#39;s in the house, we haven&#39;t found it,&quot; Pavelchik said. He said police do not believe the slayings were part of a murder-suicide.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Pavelchik said the house appeared to have been targeted but would not elaborate. &quot;I don&#39;t believe it was a random act,&quot; he told reporters.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Earlier, the police chief said &quot;the neighborhood is not in danger ... It doesn&#39;t appear there&#39;s a suspect running around the neighborhood.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Friends described the victims as loving, outgoing neighbors who went out of their way to help others.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;They were phenomenal people,&quot; said Janet Viane, who has lived next door to the Kramers for 12 years. &quot;You can&#39;t find neighbors like that.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;She said Jeffrey Kramer would throw tailgate parties in his garage at the start of every Bears season, and would help her fix her car or things around the house. Kramer ran a repair shop in Cicero, Ill.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;They&#39;re awesome parents, awesome neighbors, hard-working people,&quot; she said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The family had struggled through tragedy in 2007 when Angela was injured and her fiancee was killed while riding a motorcycle.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Angela was riding on the back of her fiancee&#39;s motorcycle when a sports utility vehicle swerved in front of them and caused them to crash, according to an employee at Kramer&#39;s Auto Repair &amp;amp; Towing.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The fiancee, Steve Hetman, was killed and Angela suffered broken legs, the employee said. &quot;I know she was very hurt in the accident and very torn up about it,&quot; he said. News reports at the time said Hetman was pinned against the SUV and Angela was thrown from the cycle.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The two had planned to marry after Hetman had found a job.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Workers at the repair shop said Jeffrey Kramer bought the business from his father, Roy Kramer, several years ago. One employee described him as a kind boss who &quot;did his best to keep us all employed&quot; during the recession.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Jeffrey Kramer was also very devoted to his family, he said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;His family came first,&quot; the worker said. &quot;I&#39;m sure it was the first thing he thought of in the morning and the last thing he thought of before he went to bed.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;A family friend, Matt Schuster, 16, said he grew up with the family and his brother was good friends with one of the sons.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Whoever killed them, he said, are &quot;sick and cold hearted. I hope they get caught and they pay for it. There&#39;s nothing this family did wrong.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;A neighbor who lives across the street, Jennifer Mazzei, said Lori Kramer worked for a textbook publisher.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;I have no idea why they would be targeted as the police said,&quot; she said. &quot;They were friendly people, outgoing. They extended themselves to us when we moved in.&quot;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;As police watched the home Tuesday morning, a distraught man ran past police tape surrounding the property before being stopped by police and turned away from the home.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The man stopped near a truck parked on the driveway and doubled over as he sobbed uncontrollably. Police walked him away from the home.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;http://thm-a01.yimg.com/nimage/6db8812693e82e54&quot; alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;This posting includes an audio/video/photo media file: &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.ihomeelevator.com/home-elevator-03.jpg&quot;&gt;Download Now&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.earthtimes.org/articles/show/adp-national-employment-report-shows,1188393.shtml&quot;&gt;ADP National Employment Report Shows U.S. Employment Decreased by 20 ... - Earthtimes&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 03 Mar 2010 05:11 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;dfont&quot;&gt;ROSELAND, NJ -- 03/03/10 -- According to today&#39;s &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.adpemploymentreport.com/&quot;&gt;ADP National Employment ReportÂ®&lt;/a&gt;, private sector employment decreased by 20,000 in February. The ADP National Employment Report, created by &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.adp.com/&quot;&gt;Automatic Data Processing, Inc. (ADPÂ®)&lt;/a&gt;, in partnership with &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.macroadvisers.com/&quot;&gt;Macroeconomic Advisers, LLC&lt;/a&gt;, is derived from actual payroll data and measures the change in total nonfarm private employment each month. &lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;pre&gt; Nonfarm Private Employment Highlights -- February Report: -- Total employment: -20,000 -- Small businesses* -18,000 -- Medium businesses** +8,000 -- Large businesses*** -10,000 -- Goods-producing sector: -37,000 -- Service-providing sector: +17,000 Addendum: &quot; Manufacturing industry: +3,000 * Small businesses represent payrolls with 1-49 employees ** Medium businesses represent payrolls with 50-499 employees *** Large businesses represent payrolls with more than 499 employees Note: all data included in the ADP National Employment Report is based on size of payroll. In some cases, small and medium-size payrolls belong to businesses employing more workers than indicated by the size grouping. &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; According to Joel Prakken, Chairman of Macroeconomic Advisers, LLC, &quot;Nonfarm private employment decreased 20,000 from January to February 2010 on a seasonally adjusted basis, according to the ADP National Employment Report. The February employment decline was the smallest since employment began falling in February of 2008. If the recent trend continues, and given first-quarter GDP growth of 5.9%, private employment could rise next month for the first time in two years.&quot; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Prakken added, &quot;In February, two large blizzards smothered parts of the east coast during the reference period for the BLS establishment survey. The adverse weather had only a very small effect on today&#39;s ADP Report due to the methodology used to construct it. However, the adverse weather is widely expected to depress the BLS estimate of the monthly change in employment for February, but boost it for March.&quot; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &quot;February&#39;s ADP Report estimates nonfarm private employment in the service-providing sector increased by 17,000, the second consecutive monthly increase. However, this employment growth was not enough to offset continued losses in the goods-producing sector. Employment in the goods-producing sector declined 37,000, with employment in the manufacturing sector increasing by 3,000. The employment increase in the manufacturing sector was the first since January 2008,&quot; said Prakken. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Prakken went on to say, &quot;Large businesses, defined as those with 500 or more workers, saw employment decline by 10,000 while small-size businesses with fewer than 50 workers, declined 18,000. Employment among medium-size businesses, defined as those with between 50 and 499 workers, increased by 8,000, the first increase in employment since January of 2008.&quot; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The matched sample used to develop the ADP National Employment Report was derived from ADP data, which during the twelve month period through December 2009, averaged over 360,000 U.S. business clients and represented over 22 million U.S. employees. This approximately represents the size of the matched sample used this month. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;pre&gt; +-------------------------------------------------------------------------+ |Notice of Annual Revisions to the ADP National Employment ReportÂ® | | | |Automatic Data Processing, Inc, in conjunction with Macroeconomic | |Advisers, LLC, has published the scheduled annual revisions to the | |estimates of employment shown in the ADP National Employment Report. This| |month&#39;s ADP Report incorporates revised historical estimates based on the| |2010 benchmark revisions to establishment employment published by the | |Bureau of Labor Statistics on February 6, 2010. The main sources of | |revision to the ADP National Employment Report are: | | | |-- Updated regression estimates used to adjust for historical differences| | in the variances of the monthly growth rates of employment reported by| | the Bureau of Labor Statistics and computed from ADP data. | |-- Updated estimates of the differences in the historical averages of the| | growth rates of employment reported by the Bureau of Labor Statistics | | and computed from ADP data. | |-- Updated estimates of historical seasonal factors. | |-- The reference month for establishing the levels of employment shown in| | the ADP National Employment Report will be advanced from March 2008 to| | March 2009. | |-- There are no revisions to the methodology of computing the estimates | | of employment shown in the ADP National Employment Report. | | | | Visit &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.adpemploymentreport.com&quot;&gt;www.adpemploymentreport.com&lt;/a&gt; for details. | +-------------------------------------------------------------------------+ &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Small Business Highlights -- February Report: &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Due to the important contribution small businesses make to economic growth, employment data that is specific to businesses with fewer than 50 employees will be reported in the &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.smallbusinessreport.adp.com/&quot;&gt;ADP Small Business Report&lt;/a&gt;Â® each month. The ADP Small Business Report is a subset of the ADP National Employment Report.* &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;pre&gt; -- Total small business employment: -18,000 -- Goods-producing sector: -25,000 small business jobs -- Service-providing sector: +7,000 small business jobs &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; *All size data included in the ADP National Employment Report is based on size of payroll. In some cases, small and medium-size payrolls belong to businesses employing more workers than indicated by the size grouping. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Private employment among &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://smallbusiness.adp.com/&quot;&gt;small businesses&lt;/a&gt; decreased by 18,000 in February, according to the ADP Small Business Report released today. Additional information about small business employment, including charts on monthly job growth and employment levels, along with historical data, is available at &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.smallbusinessreport.adp.com&quot;&gt;http://www.smallbusinessreport.adp.com&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &quot;Employment among small-size businesses, defined as those with fewer than 50 workers, declined 18,000 in February. This decline was the smallest since April of 2008. Small business employment in the service-providing sector increased by 7,000, the second consecutive monthly increase,&quot; said Joel Prakken. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; To obtain additional information about the ADP National Employment Report, including additional charts, supporting data and the schedule of future release dates, or to subscribe to the monthly e-mail alerts and RSS feeds, please visit &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.adpemploymentreport.com/&quot;&gt;www.ADPemploymentreport.com&lt;/a&gt;. The March 2010 ADP National Employment Report will be released March 31, 2010 at 8:15 A.M. ET. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; About the ADP National Employment ReportÂ® &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The ADP National Employment Report, sponsored by ADPÂ®, was developed and is maintained by Macroeconomic Advisers, LLC. It is a measure of employment derived from an anonymous subset of roughly 500,000 U.S. business clients. During the twelve month period through December 2009, this subset averaged over 360,000 U.S. business clients and over 22 million U.S. employees working in all private industrial sectors. The ADP Small Business ReportÂ® is a monthly estimate of private nonfarm employment among companies in the United States with 1-49 employees and is a subset of the ADP National Employment Report. The data for both reports is collected for pay periods that can be interpolated to include the week of the 12th of each month, and processed with statistical methodologies similar to those used by the U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics to compute employment from its monthly survey of establishments. Due to this processing, this subset is modified to make it indicative of national employment levels; therefore, the resulting employment changes computed for the ADP National Employment Report are not representative of changes in ADP&#39;s total base of U.S. business clients. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; For a description of the underlying data and the statistical properties of the series, please see &quot;ADP National Employment Report: Development Methodology&quot; at &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://adpemploymentreport.com/methodology.aspx&quot;&gt;http://ADPemploymentreport.com/methodology.aspx&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; About ADP &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; Automatic Data Processing, Inc. (NASDAQ: ADP), with nearly $9 billion in revenues and about 570,000 clients, is one of the world&#39;s largest providers of business outsourcing solutions. Leveraging 60 years of experience, ADP offers the widest range of HR, payroll, tax and benefits administration solutions from a single source. ADP&#39;s easy-to-use solutions for employers provide superior value to companies of all types and sizes. ADP is also a leading provider of integrated computing solutions to auto, truck, motorcycle, marine and recreational vehicle dealers throughout the world. (&amp;#13; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/videoshow/5634322.cms&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; Watch&amp;#13; &lt;/a&gt;&amp;#13; )&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; While&amp;#13; Maruti&#39;s sales climbed 22%, close rival Hyundai Motors posted a 43% jump,&amp;#13; its best performances in last 12 years. Tata Motors, India&#39;s biggest auto maker&amp;#13; by revenue, reported a 58% on-year surge in vehicle&amp;#13; sales.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Maruti&#39;s success was mirrored by India&#39;s second-biggest&amp;#13; two-wheeler maker, while Bajaj Auto Ltd, which reported a 78% growth in&amp;#13; motorcycle sales.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; The government had last week excise duty by 2%,&amp;#13; scrapping a waiver announced earlier as part of its booster package, and auto&amp;#13; makers immediately hiked prices by Rs 6,000 to Rs one lakh on big cars and Rs&amp;#13; 600 to Rs 2,000 on bikes. &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Officials of Maruti, Hyundai and Honda&amp;#13; said they expected a temporary slowdown in sales this month. That dip could be&amp;#13; accentuated by another imminent sales hike, say industry watchers, thanks to the&amp;#13; euro emission standards kicking in from April 1.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; But Maruti chairman&amp;#13; RC Bhargava said sales would later pick up on the back of an upbeat economy, new&amp;#13; launches and strong consumer sentiments. &quot;The sales continue on a strong pitch&amp;#13; as we have seen a lot of preponement of buying because of the anticipated rise&amp;#13; in excise duty in the Union budget during the last two months,&quot; said HMIL&amp;#13; director-sales &amp;amp; marketing Arvind Saxena. &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; Maruti, Tata, Honda&amp;#13; Siel, Mahindra &amp;amp; Mahindra, Toyota and General Motors have also increased&amp;#13; production to meet the increased demand. The pent-up demand from consumers, who&amp;#13; were waiting for new models, is also boosting sales. Some of the new launches in&amp;#13; the last few months were General Motors&#39; Beat, Toyota Etios, Ford Figo and&amp;#13; Volkswagen&#39;s Polo. &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; In January, passenger vehicles sales had&amp;#13; touched 1.83 lakh units, compared with 1.35 lakh units in January 2009.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &quot;The growth momentum, with double-digit sales growth, is&amp;#13; likely to continue this month, too. However, it may not be sustainable in the&amp;#13; long run. We expect a compounded growth rate of 10-15% and passenger vehicle&amp;#13; volumes to touch 3.5 million units in 2015,&quot; said Rakesh Batra, partner&amp;#13; and national director for auto practice at consulting firm Ernst &amp;amp;&amp;#13; Young.&amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 02 Mar 2010 08:04 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;lingo_span&quot; class=&quot;lingo_region&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;p&gt;WINSTON-SALEM, N.C. -- &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Ownership of the GMAC Insurance property and casualty division has been fully transferred to American Capital Acquisition Corp, the company said Tuesday.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;GMAC Insurance Personal Lines, which includes automobile, commercial vehicle, motorcycle and RV insurance offerings, will continue to operate as it had and its headquarters will remain in Winston-Salem, N.C.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The new CEO is Larry Pentis, who joined GMAC Insurance from The Commerce Group, where he ran all operations outside of Massachusetts. Effective immediately, he takes over CEO duties from interim executive Mary Hennessey.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;GMAC Insurance Personal Lines has retained the right to use the name GMAC Insurance in association with its remaining insurance operations while a strategic review of all brand marketing is conducted.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;GMAC Insurance Personal Lines has operated continually since 1925. It includes a network of over 10,000 independent agents and brokers in 47 states and the District of Columbia.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The GMAC Insurance Dealer Products &amp;amp; Services group and other international personal lines insurance operations remain a part of GMAC Financial Services.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;American Capital Acquisition Corp., is a newly formed corporation. The principal was a founder of AmTrust Financial Services Inc. and Maiden Holdings Ltd.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;i&gt;Copyright 2009 Associated Press. All rights reserved. &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 02 Mar 2010 06:16 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spacer8&quot;&gt;Â &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;grey11&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Tuesday, March 2, 2010&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text18&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;AMA Pro Racing Announces Enhanced Purse for Auto Club Speedway&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spacer8&quot;&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;320&quot; height=&quot;1&quot; align=&quot;center&quot;/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spacer8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;spacer8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;p align=&quot;left&quot;&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;intelliTxt&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text12&quot;&gt;DAYTONA BEACH, Fla. -- AMA Pro Racing officials announced today that the overall purse for the March 26-28 road racing event at Auto Club Speedway will feature added financial benefits for riders in the AMA Pro National Guard American SuperBike class.&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;The top three finishers in AMA Pro National Guard American SuperBike will now receive additional money and prize money that will be paid down to 15th place.&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&quot;We are pleased to add to the AMA Pro National Guard American SuperBike prize fund,&quot; said David Atlas, Chief Operating Officer of AMA Pro Racing, &quot;the competition this year is extremely close and with the added financial incentives, the racing will be better than ever.&quot;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;This year&#39;s National Guard American SuperBike field is lead by Josh Hayes (Team Graves Yamaha), Tommy Hayden (Rockstar Makita Suzuki), Larry Pegram (Foremost Insurance Ducati), Ben Bostrom (Pat Clark Motorsports Yamaha) and AMA Pro Racing returnee John Hopkins (M4 Monster Energy Suzuki). Joining Hayes, Bostrom and Hayden as former winners at Auto Club Speedway are Aaron Yates (Jordan Motorsports Suzuki), Jake Zemke (National Guard Suzuki), making this one of the most competitive fields in years. &lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;The purse structures for the AMA Pro Racing Daytona SportBike presented by AMSOIL and the AMA Pro SuperSport classes will remain as announced with Daytona SportBike prize monies being paid from 1st to 20th places and SuperSport paying 1st through 10th places. &lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;For tickets and track information, please check www.autoclubspeedway.com . Also visit www.amaproracing.com for the latest AMA Pro Racing results and information.&lt;br/&gt;AMA Pro Racing is the premier professional motorcycle racing organization in North America, operating a full schedule of events and championships for a variety of motorcycle disciplines. Learn more about AMA Pro Racing at www.amaproracing.com.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;4&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.theautochannel.com/F/news/2010/03/02/467635.html&quot;&gt;Car Wreck - An Expose Of The Auto Industry - The Auto Chanel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 02 Mar 2010 07:49 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;article-text&quot;&gt;&lt;br clear=&quot;all&quot;/&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br clear=&quot;all&quot;/&gt;  &lt;/p&gt;&lt;i&gt;&quot;I know you&#39;re angry. I helped make you that way. I was a car dealer for twelve years... And I am going to teach you all the things you&#39;d never know about the car business by telling you all the things I shouldn&#39;t. The stuff you would never see on TV news...&quot; &lt;/i&gt; &lt;p&gt;By &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt; Mark Ragsdale&lt;/a&gt; &lt;br/&gt;Author / Speaker / Trainer / Consultant&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Are consumers angry at the car business? You bet! Do they have good reason to be? Sure! Failing to get enough for their trade-in to even cover their current auto loan, getting sucked in on advertisements for which they mysteriously don&#39;t qualify, and paying up to hundreds more per month than they anticipated, without a receiving credible explanation why are reason enough. Most consumers end up driving home something other than their first choice of automobile and paying more than they expected for it. Why?&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;For much of the last half-century, frustration toward the car business over stories like these lived no farther away than your office water cooler, local pub, or Sunday barbecue. If you ever questioned the driving forces behind the anguish of car buying, read this series of articles I am developing for TheAutoChannel.com. If you were ever curious about the real goings-on behind the guarded walls of the automobile industry, you will find the answers right here. If you work somewhere in the automobile industry; from the assembly line, to the dealership delivery lane, or in the banking industry underwriting all this madnessâThe AutoChannel.com will spell it all out for you.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;As I condense and serialize my new book Car Wreck: How You Got Rear-Ended, Run Over, &amp;amp; Crushed by the U.S. Auto Industry, not only will you be better equipped to protect your wallet as a consumer, but I will also make you the resident auto industry expert within your circle of friends. While others postulate and theorize you will know the inside story behind the industry: why it is currently failing and how it can be fixed. Think of this Auto Channel series as your secret decoder ring into a subject everyone guesses about but few truly understand.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;How do I know you are angry and confused? I helped make you that way. I was a car dealer for twelve years, owning six franchised auto dealerships and three franchised motorcycle stores. I have been banging around dealerships since the age of seven. And I am going to teach you all the things you&#39;d never know about the car business by telling you all the things I shouldn&#39;t. The stuff you would never see on TV news. A fair warning is in order though. What I have to say may anger you even more.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;I am a messenger of truth, but no angel. I consummated car deals I knew in my heart were not in the best interest of my customers, deals I would not have made if I were sitting on their side of the table. I was neither their clergyman, nor their financial advisor, but a car dealer trying to score as big a profit possible. Profit is not a four-letter word. However, nothing I ever did, or any other dealer might legally do, could rival the rear-ending you are taking by not knowing what you don&#39;t know.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;There are dozens of books that can guide you on how to negotiate your best price at a car dealership. I hope they are helpful to you. Negotiating with professional negotiators can be a scary endeavor. Manufacturers, banks, unions and the government love when a new one of these consumer guides hits the shelves. It keeps them out of the limelight. As you chase after an extra thousand dollars or so in savings at the dealership level, these institutions manipulate the market value of your trade-in, keep you in debt, reduce your credit rating, and altogether prevent you from driving what you would otherwise be able to afford. They operate with little or no oversight; flying under the radar, using the public face of car dealers to hide their indiscretions.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;There are reasons why you owe more on the vehicle you drive than it is worth. There are reasons why your car payment goes up each time you trade for an essentially equivalent model. One thing I know for sure, dealer profit is not the cause. You have far bigger fish to fry than purchasing your next car or truck at dealer cost. I say this with absolute assuredness, regardless of your personal wealth, income, debt, or credit situation. No matter who you are, I&#39;m talking to you.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Protecting your self-interests requires arming yourself with the inside truth. Opinions provided by someone sitting in a boardroom or behind a news bureau desk no longer count. Shell games and perpetuated misconceptions have no room here. The industry has commanded $63 billion in taxpayer bailouts. A government task force has nuked some 2,150-car dealerships off the map. The casualties of their unfettered actions include thousands of otherwise profitable businesses (and their employees) now forced into bankruptcy! Apparently they are not &quot;too big to fail,&quot; in the eyes of our politicians. In the meantime, you have unwittingly funded the handcuffs of having fewer places to shop, fewer vehicles in stock to compare, and less price competition in the marketplace.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Dealers are solely responsible for delivering all the automobiles ever to be built in this country. They do so, while being maligned by extreme bias in the American pop culture. They endure the latest whims of their automakers&#39; management, while stroking adulterous relationships with fickle, fair-weather bankers. They navigate senseless legislation that gains votes for bill sponsors, but hinders commerce and hobbles the economy. These Trojan horse laws are designed to look pretty enough on the outside. But they serve as nothing more than smoke screens hiding the real issuesâthose that rear-end you, run you over, and crush you the quickest.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We have set the table and truth is on its way over for dinner. In the next of our series, I will cover the language car salespeople use, why they use it, and how you can leverage your newly found translating skills to get a better deal. At the end of the day, I want to shorten the amount of time you need to spend at the dealership. Get in, get a car, and get out will be our mantra. Because just like sitting in the dentist&#39;s chair, more time usually equals more pain.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.MarkRagsdale.com&quot;&gt;www.MarkRagsdale.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span&gt;Email&lt;/span&gt;: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:Mark@MarkRagsdale.com&quot;&gt;Mark@MarkRagsdale.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span&gt;Business Phone&lt;/span&gt;: 508.299.7080&lt;br/&gt;&lt;span&gt;Fax&lt;/span&gt;: 866.299.6010&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;span&gt;Author&#39;s Social Media Contacts:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt; Facebook Author Page: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.facebook.com/CarWreckBook&quot;&gt;www.facebook.com/CarWreckBook&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt; Twitter Author Page: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.twitter.com/MarkRagsdale&quot;&gt;www.twitter.com/MarkRagsdale&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt; LinkedIn Profile: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.linkedin.com/in/MarkRagsdale&quot;&gt;www.linkedin.com/in/MarkRagsdale&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;span&gt;Car Wreck&#39;s Social Media Contacts:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br/&gt; Facebook Fan Page: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.facebook.com/CarWreckFans&quot;&gt;www.facebook.com/CarWreckFans&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt; Twitter Book Page: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.twitter.com/CarWreckBook&quot;&gt;www.twitter.com/CarWreckBook&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;p&gt;Mark Ragsdale is author of the book Car Wreck: How You Got Rear-Ended, Run Over, &amp;amp; Crushed by the U.S. Auto Industry (Langdon Street Press, ISBN-13: 978-1934938652, Paperback 256 pp., $15.95). It is sold by booksellers nationwide and online. Mark has been interviewed by Fox Business Channel&#39;s Neil Cavuto, Wall Street Journal Radio, and various syndicated news columnists. &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;table id=&quot;itemcontentlist&quot;&gt; &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://biz.yahoo.com/prnews/100301/30002566en_uspublic.html?.v=1&quot;&gt;TAAP Data Capture Mobile Software Triumphs at MCN Show - Yahoo Finance&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 28 Feb 2010 11:58 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;y-article-bd&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;BOREHAMWOOD, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;England&lt;/span&gt;, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-chron&quot;&gt;March 1, 2010&lt;/span&gt; /PRNewswire/ -- Triumph - the largest British automotive manufacturer, producing around 50,000 motorcycles a year - used TAAP&#39;s Data Capture mobile software on a rental basis to collect leads at the recent Motorcycle News (MCN) show. With a comprehensive network of professional dealerships, Triumph offers test rides throughout the UK. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; The MCN show is the biggest annual motorcycle show in the &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;London&lt;/span&gt;/South East area, with people travelling from outside the UK to attend. TAAP - a leading mobile software application provider with significant expertise in the automotive sector - provided Triumph with eight PDA devices (handheld mobile computers) for use at the show, held at the Excel centre from 4th - &lt;span class=&quot;xn-chron&quot;&gt;7th February 2010&lt;/span&gt;. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; TAAP&#39;s award-winning Data Capture application operates via Pocket PCs/PDAs to allow Triumph to collect customer data and view it in real-time on a secure website, completely eliminating paper forms. This makes remote event management and tracking much easier as information is immediately visible. Data is securely managed as it is encrypted on the device and when sent from it. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Emphasizing its flexible approach to software customisation, TAAP provided Triumph with a &#39;nearest dealer&#39; feature. This ensured that when customers were contacted at a later date with regards to a test ride, this would be done by their nearest Triumph dealer. The application includes mandatory fields which ensure that all leads collected contain uniform information in a set format, and missing data is a thing of the past. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Triumph were pleased with the ease of use of the application and the quality of the lead data captured, and confirmed further use of the technology for the forthcoming Scottish MCN event organised by Live Promotions and held at the Royal Highland Centre, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-location&quot;&gt;Edinburgh&lt;/span&gt; on 20th and &lt;span class=&quot;xn-chron&quot;&gt;21st March 2010&lt;/span&gt;. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Triumph account manager at TAAP, &lt;span class=&quot;xn-person&quot;&gt;Louise Lawson&lt;/span&gt;, said &quot;We&#39;re delighted that Triumph found the Data Capture application a success and are planning to use it again for the Scottish show. Secure data collection through the TAAP mobile software means customers benefit from a more accurate and far quicker response.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; About Data Capture &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; TAAP Data Capture enables secure collection of data whilst out of the office on a mobile device. Further details are available at: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.ontaap.com/TAAPDataCapture.aspx&quot; class=&quot;yltasis&quot;&gt;http://www.ontaap.com/TAAPDataCapture.aspx&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; About TAAP &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; TAAP is a leading provider of software solutions which allow organisations to mobilise their operations using hand held computers. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p/&gt;&lt;pre&gt; Contact TAAP Tel: +44(0)845-230-9787 Email: angela.walker@ontaap.com Website: http://www.ontaap.com &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.thepeninsulaqatar.com/Display_news.asp?section=Business_News&amp;subsection=market+news&amp;month=March2010&amp;file=Business_News20100301112921.xml&quot;&gt;Toyota recall woes said to lie in cost-cutting - Peninsula&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 01 Mar 2010 12:41 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;b&gt;Toyota recall woes said to lie in cost-cutting&lt;/b&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;br/&gt;Web posted at: 3/1/2010 11:29:21&lt;br/&gt;&amp;#13; Source ::: WP-Bloomberg&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;By Alan Ohnsman, Jeff Green and Kae Inoue&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;KKatsuaki Watanabe, Toyotas former president, did something at his first meeting with US investors out of character for a leader of Japans biggest carmaker: He boasted of what hed accomplished. On the job as Toyotas chief executive for less than three months, Watanabe told New Yorks financial community at the September 12, 2005, gathering that a cost-reduction programme he designed had wrung out more than $10bn of savings over six years. Called Construction of Cost Competitiveness in the 21st Century, the initiative was only a start, he said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Under CCC21 activities, which I led, Toyota realised cost reductions of more than 200bn yen ($2.2bn) a year on a consolidated basis, Watanabe said. Next was an aggressive version of CCC21 Watanabe called Value Innovation that promised more savings by making the entire development process cheaper and further trimming parts and production costs.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The programmes, a steroid shot to Toyotas trademark kaizen approach of steady, gradual cost reduction, were blessed by its board and investors attracted after Toyota listed shares in New York and London in 1999. An obsession with cost reductions and rapid growth help explain how a company long revered for quality is under fire from US legislators and lawyers amid recalls of 8.5 million autos worldwide.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The root cause of their problems is that the company was hijacked, some years ago, by anti-(Toyoda) family, financially oriented pirates, said Jim Press, Toyotas former US chief and only American to hold a seat on the companys board.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Those executives, whom Press didnt identify, didnt have the character necessary to maintain a customer first focus, he said. Press left the company in 2007 after an unwanted job transfer. All automakers are focused on reducing cost, said Jim Wiseman, Toyotas vice president for North American corporate communications.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Its not true that by reducing cost you automatically reduce quality, Wiseman said. Every automaker has to stay competitive relative to price.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Watanabe, now a vice chairman for Toyota, declined to be interviewed for this story, Mieko Iwasaki, a company spokeswoman said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The worlds largest carmaker has lost $32.6bn in market value since a January 21 recall to fix gas pedals that can stick. That followed a recall for accelerator pedals that can be trapped by floor mats and cause unwanted acceleration.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Its also adding braking software on millions of recalled and future vehicles to help stop unintended speed-ups and adjusting brake programming on the Prius and other hybrids.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The company also faces at least 84 class action lawsuits involving sudden acceleration and at least 25 individual cases filed in courts in the U.S. and Canada. &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Toyota said in a regulatory filing this week it received subpoenas from a federal grand jury in the Southern District of New York on February 8 and the Los Angeles office of the Securities and Exchange Commission on February 19 for documents related to potential product defects.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Watanabe, trained as an economist, not as an engineer, also said at the New York conference that the Japan-based company was able to slash time to bring models into production once a design was final to about 12 months, compared with an industry average of between 24 and 36 months.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The shorter production time enables us to develop a variety of vehicles that reflect market needs and demands while fulfilling the advanced development structure, Watanabe said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Akio Toyoda, who succeeded Watanabe in June 2009, acknowledged this week that such changes may have contributed to product defects. I fear the pace at which we have grown may have been too quick, Toyoda, whose grandfather founded the company in 1937, said on Wednesday at a congressional hearing in Washington. Priorities became confused, and we were not able to stop, think and make improvements as much as we were able to before.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Even before unintended acceleration leading to driver deaths cast an unwanted spotlight on the company, Toyoda told investors he had become concerned about the companys fixation with growth and boosting profit.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last September, at a meeting with Toyota investors near the Tokyo Dome, home to the Yomiuri Giants professional baseball team, Toyoda said growth goals had hurt the company, according to an executive who was present.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Under Watanabe, Toyota had three consecutive record years, with net income rising from $15.3m in fiscal 2006, his first year as president, to $19.3m in fiscal 2008. In fiscal 2009, with collapsing sales brought on by a global financial crisis, Watanabe also oversaw a $49bn net loss, the worst in company history.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;At a 2006 investor conference in London Watanabe and former Executive Vice President Kazuo Okamoto discussed plans to exceed the cost-reduction results achieved in CCC21 by eliminating vehicle parts and pushing suppliers to adopt lighter, cheaper materials.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;While the programmes brought development advances, they may have inadvertently triggered quality glitches, said current and former company officials who asked not to be named because the information isnt public.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For models such as the Camry, that led to an expectation that each new part on the top-selling US passenger car be at least 10 percent cheaper and 10 percent lighter than the one it replaced, said an official at a supplier who asked not to be named as the person still works with Toyota.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Problems with Camry were evident during production of a redesigned model in February 2006, said a supplier executive who worked directly on the program who asked not to be named as the persons current employer still does business with Toyota.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The new vehicle had a flaw in the design of the headliner, the fabric and composite lining that covers the inside roof of the car, which led to almost a third of the parts being ruined during production, the executive said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Sweeping cost-cutting programs arent unique to Toyota. Honda recently started the C8G3 program for motorcycle parts procurement, according to Executive Vice President Koichi Kondo.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The program, which doesnt have a concrete timeline, aims to consolidate global procurement to three suppliers for 80 percent of parts to reduce costs, Kondo said. Hondas auto segment may also employ a similar program, said spokeswoman Natsuno Asanuma.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Toyotas use of large-scale cost reduction programs didnt end after Watanabe stepped down last year, the company said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The former chief executives Value Innovation plan has been succeeded by a program known internally as RRCI, said Hideaki Homma, a company spokesman. Toyota met with suppliers on December 21 to outline the initiative, Homma said.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;While Akio Toyoda vowed to revamp Toyotas tarnished image and repair internal processes warped by mistakes of the past decade, actions of previous leaders echo a comment by his great- uncle Eiji Toyoda.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Water can be wrung even from a dry towel if you put your mind to it, said Eiji Toyoda, a former company president, when describing how Toyota slashed costs after the 1973 Oil Crisis.&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. href=&quot;http://www.newkerala.com/news/fullnews-61228.html&quot;&gt;TVS posts 31 per cent growth in sales in February 2010 - New Kerala&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 28 Feb 2010 11:22 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;KonaBody&quot;&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;b&gt;Mumbai, Mar 1 : Post an alround growth TVS Motor Company today reported a 31 per cent increase in its sales in February in the two wheeler segment at 140,544 units as against 107,301 sold in February 2009.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The Company in a release here said the growth for the year to date was 14 per cent at 1.37 million vehicles sold as against 1.20 million sold during the corresponding period of last fiscal.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;TVS Motor in a release here said the three wheeler sales also posted sizeable growth over February 2009, generating highest ever sales. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Domestic sales posted growth of 34 per cent registering 121,403 units in February 2010 in comparison with 90,718 units in the February 2009. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The company&#39;s motorcycle registered a buoyant growth of 28 per cent in February 2010 with sales of 63,394 units in February 2010 when compared to 49,659 units in the same month of the previous year. During the month, scooters witnessed substantial growth of 38 per cent registering sales of 27,017 units when compared to 19,532 units in February 2009. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Exports continued to show an upward trend posting 15 per cent during the month of February with sales of 19,141 units against 16,583 units in February 2009. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The company recorded 2,132 units of three wheeler sales in February 2010 against 550 units in February 2009; cumulative sales for the period April 2009 to February 2010 thus adding up to 12,549 units. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;During the month, &#39;TVS Jive&#39;, India&#39;s first auto clutch motorcycle was introduced in markets across Tamilnadu as well as Andhra Pradesh. The bike will be made available in phases across the country within the next month. The company will also launch its much awaited TVS Wego in phases across the country beginning this month. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p align=&quot;left&quot;&gt; --UNI&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;div id=&quot;bestofcont&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 28 Feb 2010 09:21 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;content&quot; id=&quot;bd&quot;&gt; &lt;i&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://www.prlog.org&quot;&gt;PR Log (Press Release)&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt; â &lt;i&gt;Mar 01, 2010&lt;/i&gt; â Roadkill Enterprises has launched a new website ( http://www.VehicleWars.com ) that pits cars, trucks, hot rods, motorcycles, race cars and many other vehicle types against each other in head-to-head competitions. Visitors can rate each vehicle in a head-to-head, side-by-side format on a scale of 1 to 10 and vote for their winner in each completion, or battle. &amp;#13;&lt;p&gt;Registered members can upload photos of their vehicles to participate in the head-to-head battles that can span all categories, mixed categories, or specific vehicle types. Members can upload an unlimited number of vehicles and manage them and view battle statistics via My Vehicles web site interface. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Statistics are tracked for each member&#39;s individual vehicles, as well as each member&#39;s collective statistics. Overall statistics are also compiled so that members can see how they are doing across all of the vehicles on the site. &amp;#13;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Registration for the site is free and we operate under a strict no-spam policy. &lt;div xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml&quot; id=&quot;emailbody&quot; style=&quot;margin:0 2em;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt; &lt;table style=&quot;border:0;padding:0;margin:0;width:100%&quot;&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;vertical-align:top&quot; width=&quot;99%&quot;&gt; &lt;h1 style=&quot;margin:0;padding-bottom:6px;&quot;&gt; title=&quot;(http://pipes.yahoo.com/pipes/pipe.info?_id=GLEvgE153BGfQ1cmEpPZnA)&quot;&gt;plus 3, New Bosch motorcycle ABS prevents up to 48% of fatal accidents - The Auto Chanel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;br /&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;http://fusion.google.com/add?source=atgs&amp;amp;feedurl=http://feeds.feedburner.com/yahoo/FHQZ&quot;&gt; &lt;img style=&quot;padding-top:6px&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; src=&quot;http://gmodules.com/ig/images/plus_google.gif&quot; /&gt; &lt;/a&gt; &lt;/h1&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;td width=&quot;1%&quot; /&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;/table&gt; &lt;hr style=&quot;border:1px solid #ccc;padding:0;margin:0&quot; /&gt; &lt;ul style=&quot;clear:both;padding:0 0 0 1.2em;width:100%&quot; id=&quot;summarylist&quot;&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#1&quot;&gt;New Bosch motorcycle ABS prevents up to 48% of fatal accidents - The Auto Chanel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#2&quot;&gt;BoI approves new auto dev&amp;rsquo;t program - Manila Bulleting Online&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#3&quot;&gt;Patch not an issue at DIS - Daytona Beach News-Journal&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#4&quot;&gt;MARCH CALENDAR - Dallas Morning News&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;table id=&quot;itemcontentlist&quot;&gt; &lt;tr xmlns=&quot;&quot;&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.theautochannel.com/F/news/2010/02/28/467348.html&quot;&gt;New Bosch motorcycle ABS prevents up to 48% of fatal accidents - The Auto Chanel&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 28 Feb 2010 04:46 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;article-text&quot;&gt;&lt;br clear=&quot;all&quot;/&gt;&lt;p&gt;Auto Central February 28th, 2010; Bosch has recently developed a new generation antilock braking system (ABS) for motorcycles which has the potential to prevent 38 per cent of motorcycle accidents involving personal injury and 48 per cent of those leading to fatalities, according to a study published by the Swedish highways authority. Further, a study published by the German Federal Highway Research Institute (BASt) concludes that fatality rates would be reduced by 12 per cent if all motorcycles were equipped with ABS. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The lightweight, cost-optimized system developed by Bosch has received the &#39;Innovation and Environment&#39; award from Germany-based ADAC, Europe&#39;s largest automobile club, making Bosch the third time recipient of this award since 2005. The pioneering equipment weighs only 0.7 kilograms, features a cost-effective design, and is half the size and weight of previous motorcycle ABS systems made by Bosch. It is part of a new Bosch modular generation which was introduced in November 2009. All other ABS systems currently on the market are based on passenger-car technology. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&quot;This new system has the potential to greatly advance road safety initiatives throughout the Middle East, which has a strong base of motorcycling enthusiasts,&quot; said Volker Bischoff, General Manager, Robert Bosch ME. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Although the Middle East in general has a high incidence of road accidents, Saudi traffic authorities say that fatalities in the Kingdom have been decreasing since 2004 due to improved traffic laws. Motorcycle accidents in particular occur due mainly to poor driving experience and night driving with poor illumination. The introduction of new technologies such as Bosch&#39;s new braking system would perfectly complement the government&#39;s enforcement of stricter motorcycling laws. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The active safety mechanism used by the new Bosch product enables motorcyclists to brake safely in emergency situations without locking their wheels and significantly reduces braking distance. Only every tenth new motorcycle manufactured in Europe adopts this kind of system, while on a global scale only every one-hundredth is equipped. In comparison, around 80 per cent of passenger cars worldwide use it. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Bosch has been manufacturing brake control systems for motorcycles since 1994. Its new ABS system was designed by engineers at the company&#39;s competence center in Japan. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; About Bosch: &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Bosch Group is a leading global supplier of technology and services. According to preliminary figures, some 270,000 associates generated sales of roughly 38 billion euros in the areas of automotive and industrial technology, consumer goods, and building technology in fiscal 2009. The Bosch Group comprises Robert Bosch GmbH and its more than 300 subsidiaries and regional companies in over 60 countries. If its sales and service partners are included, then Bosch is represented in roughly 150 countries. This worldwide development, manufacturing, and sales network is the foundation for further growth. Each year, Bosch spends more than 3.5 billion euros for research and development, and applies for over 3,000 patents worldwide. With all its products and services, Bosch enhances the quality of life by providing solutions which are both innovative and beneficial. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The company was set up in Stuttgart in 1886 by Robert Bosch (1861-1942) as &quot;Workshop for Precision Mechanics and Electrical Engineering.&quot; The special ownership structure of Robert Bosch GmbH guarantees the entrepreneurial freedom of the Bosch Group, making it possible for the company to plan over the long term and to undertake significant up-front investments in the safeguarding of its future. Ninety-two percent of the share capital of Robert Bosch GmbH is held by Robert Bosch Stiftung GmbH, a charitable foundation. The majority of voting rights are held by Robert Bosch Industrietreuhand KG, an industrial trust. The entrepreneurial ownership functions are carried out by the trust. The remaining shares are held by the Bosch family and by Robert Bosch GmbH. http://www.bosch.com/&amp;gt; &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;2&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.mb.com.ph/articles/245525/boi-approves-new-auto-dev-t-program&quot;&gt;BoI approves new auto dev&amp;rsquo;t program - Manila Bulleting Online&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 28 Feb 2010 01:40 AM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;content clear-block&quot;&gt;&amp;#13;  &lt;p&gt;The Board of Investments (BoI) has finally approved the new Motor Vehicle Development Program (MVDP), an industry blueprint that aims to improve the competitiveness of the country&#39;s auto sector which has been lagging behind other ASEAN countries.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Trade and Industry Undersecretary and BoI Elmer C. Hernandez said the prepared Executive Order entitled &quot;Providing for a New Comprehensive Motor Vehicle Industry Development Policy and Direction,&quot; has been submitted to Secretary Peter B. Favila, who will endorse it to President Gloria Arroyo for signing.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&quot;We incorporated most comments from the automotive players in the EO. It is now up to Secretary Favila when to endorse it to MalacaÃ±ang for the president&#39;s signature,&quot; Hernandez said.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;As this developed, auto players are now bracing for the preparation of the implementing rules and regulations of the new MVDP, which are expected to be more contentious than in the preparation of the MVDP.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The implementing rules and regulations of the MVDP would spell out into specific measures the program&#39;s general provisions like the creation of the powerful automotive council, incentives, exports program, importation of used motor vehicles, standards, among others.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;On the establishment of the Automotive Industry Development Council as a policy making body of the industry attached to the BoI, the Chamber of Automotive Manufacturers of the Philippines Inc. has already opposed its creation stating they would rather maintain a status quo where the industry is under the BoI.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The creation of the Council calls for the upgrading of the Motor Vehicles Division of the BoI to a Department to be called Motor Vehicle Industry Department under the BoI with a manpower complement of at least 20 technical and clerical personnel.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;The BoI shall submit a supplemental budget to the Department of Budget and Management, which shall set aside an initial amount of P20 million. Thereafter, the Council shall have a budgetary allocation from the General Appropriations Act under the BoI budget.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Article 2 of the proposed EO is a carry over from the old MVDP covering program components (passenger cars, commercial vehicles and motorcycles), the program participants, investment requirements and privileges.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Article 3 of the EO is entirely devoted to the prohibition on the importation of used motor vehicles. But, while Section 1 of Article 3 prohibits the importation into the country of all types of used motor vehicles, it also allows enough room for their entry.&lt;/p&gt;  &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. Available tools: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/pdf-newspaper/&quot;&gt;PDF Newspaper&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/content-only/&quot;&gt;Full Text RSS&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org/term-extraction/&quot;&gt;Term Extraction&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;image&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/td&gt; &lt;/tr&gt; &lt;tr&gt; &lt;td style=&quot;margin-bottom:0;line-height:1.4em;&quot;&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;margin:1em 0 3px 0;&quot;&gt; &lt;a name=&quot;3&quot; style=&quot;font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;font-size:18px;&quot; href=&quot;http://www.news-journalonline.com/racing/other/2010/02/28/patch-not-an-issue-at-dis.html&quot;&gt;Patch not an issue at DIS - Daytona Beach News-Journal&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/p&gt; &lt;p style=&quot;font-size:13px;color:#555;margin:9px 0 3px 0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;Posted:&lt;/span&gt; 27 Feb 2010 11:16 PM PST&lt;/p&gt; &lt;div style=&quot;margin:0;font-family:Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,Sans-Serif;line-height:140%;font-size:13px;color:#FFFFFF;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;asset-body&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; &amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;DAYTONA BEACH -- The tiny pothole that brought the mighty Daytona 500 to its knees has been eliminated as a racing nuisance. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;The hole, which started as a gouge from the chassis of a Sprint Cup Series stock car, caused NASCAR to stop the 500 twice for more than 2 1/2 hours to repair the area. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;The pothole was fixed with a concrete patch four days after the checkered flag fell on the Daytona 500, capping three weeks of auto racing events. The area was allowed to &quot;cure&quot; for several days to complete the repair. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Daytona 200 Motorcycle Week started Saturday with a dozen motorcycle road-racing events and the patch was not a worry for competitors. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;There have been no issues with the bikes,&quot; Speedway president Robin Braig said. &quot;We talked to tire and bike manufacturers and riders and there are no concerns.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;In a random survey of Championship Cup Series riders, who are racing in the West Banking area, the consensus was the patch -- closer to the apron than the outside retaining wall -- was not even in the preferred racing line. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;The higher you run, the better because there&#39;s less wind resistance,&quot; Bonita Springs rider Charles Long said. &quot;That patch really has no effect. You can see it because it&#39;s a lighter gray than the rest of the track.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;David Loikits, Allentown, Pa., a Speedway &#39;Cycle Week veteran, said he noticed the patch &quot;on the cool down lap&quot; after his race on Saturday. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;It&#39;s not an issue at all,&quot; Loikits said. &quot;It&#39;s no big deal. Nobody has complained about it at all.&quot; &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;Braig is confident the patch will serve its purpose. &lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;p&gt;&quot;We don&#39;t anticipate any other issues with our track surface,&quot; Braig said.&lt;/p&gt;&amp;#13; &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;mailto:godwin.kelly@news-jrnl.com&quot;&gt;&amp;#13; godwin.kelly&amp;#13; @news-jrnl.com&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#13; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://fivefilters.org&quot;&gt;Five Filters&lt;/a&gt; featured article: &lt;a rel=&quot;nofollow&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; href=&quot;http://medialens.org/alerts/09/091216_chilcot_inquiry_the.php&quot;&gt;Chilcot Inquiry&lt;/a&gt;. &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#1&quot;&gt;Mobile drives emphasize importance of blood donations - Chillico Gazette&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;a href=&quot;#2&quot;&gt;There is some hope for a drag strip in Mansfield - Bucyrus Telegraph Forum&lt;/a&gt;
